KSB 1 (Dickins)
B18.1.
Cambridge, Corpus Christi College, MS. 383: Dickins 1952, 2-4.



 1. Þa wæs agangen fram Cristes acennednesse cccc & xciiii
wintra, þa Cerdic & Cynric his sunu coman up æt Cerdices oran mid fif
scipun.
 4. Ond se Cerdic wes elesing.
 4. Elesa gewising.
 4. Gewis wiging.
 5. Wig freawining.
 5. Frawine freoðagaring.
 6. Freoðagar bronding.
 6. Brond beldæging.
 7. Beldæg woldening.
 7. Þes ymb vi gear þes ðe hy up coman hy geeodan westseaxna
rice & þæt wæron þa ærestan cynegas þe westseaxna land on
wealdum geeodon.
 10. Ond he hæfde þæt rice xvi gear, þa he gefor.
 11. Þa feng Cynric his sunu to þam rice & heold xxvi
wintra.
 13. Þa he forðferde þa feng Ceaulin his sunu to & heold
vii gear, þa he gefor.
 14. Þa feng Ceolulf to his broðor & he ricsode xvii gear.
 16. Heora cyn geð to Cerdice.
 16. Þa feng Cynegils Ceolwulfes broðorsunu to rice & heold
xxxi wintra, & he onfeng ærest fulwihte westseaxna cyninga.
 19. & þa feng Cenwealh to & heold xxxi wintra & se
Cenwalh wæs Cynegilses sunu.
 21. Ond þa heold seaxburh his cwen an gear þæt rice æfter
him.
 22. Þa feng æscwine to rice þes cyn gæð to Cerdice.
 23. Ond he heold ii gear.
 24. Þa feng Centwine.

END_TEXT
START_TEXT

KSB 2 (Sweet)
B18.2.
London, British Library, MS. Add. 23211: Sweet 1885, 179.



 1. Rice & heold xxxvii wint, & vii monað, ond ða feng
æðelwulf his sunu to, & heold xviiii healf gear, ond se æðelwulf
wæs ecgberhting, ecgberht ealhcmunding, ealhmund eabing, eaba eopping, eoppa
ingilding, ingild coenreding, coenred ceolwalding, ceolwald cuðuulfing,
cuðuulf cuðwining, cuðwine ceaulniing, ceaulin cynnricing, cynnric
crioding, criodo ceardicing, ond ða feng æðelbald his sunu to, &
heold v gear, ða feng æðelberht his broðor to rice, & heold v
gear, ða feng æðered his broðor to rice, & heold v gear, ða feng
ælfred hira broðar to rice, ond ða wæs agan his eldo xxiii wintra,
ond ccc ond xcvi wintra ðæs ðe his cynn ærest westseaxna bond on
walum geeodon.
 12. <foreign>de regibus orientalium seaxonum</foreign>.
 13. Offa sighering, sighere sigberhting, sigberht sawearding,
saweard saberhting, saberht sledding, sledd æscwining, æscwine offing,
offa bedcing, bedca sigefugling, sigefugl swæpping, swæppa antsecging,
antsecg gesecging, gesecg seaxneting.
 17. <foreign>item de regibus orientalium seaxonum</foreign>.
 18. Swiðred sigemunding, sigemund sigeharding, sigehard sebbing,
sebbe seaxreding, seaxred saberhting, saberht sledding.
 20. <foreign>item de regibus orientalium seoxonum</foreign>.
 21. Sigered sigericing, sigeric selereding, selered sigeberhting,
sigeberht sigebalding, sigebald seleferðing, seleferð sigeferðing,
sigeferð seaxing, seaxa sledding, ðonan forð.

KSB 3 (Nap)
B18.3.
London, British Library, MS. Add. 34652, fol. 2: Napier 1897, 105-11.



 1. Þy geare þe wæs agan fram cristes acennednesse feower
hund wintra & feower & hundnygenti wintra þa cerdic & cinric his
sunu cuomon up æt cerdices oran mid fif scypum.
 5. & se cerdic wæs elesing, Elesa Esling, Esla Gewising,
Gewis Wiging, Wig Freawining, Freawine Friþugaring, Friþugar Bronding,
Brond Bældæging, Bældæg Wodening.
 10. Ond þæs ymb syx gear þæs þe hy up cuomon geeodon
westseaxna rice & þæt wærun þa ærestan cyningas þe wesseaxna
lond on wealum geeodon & he hæfde þæt rice syx gear & þa he
gefor.
 15. Þa feng his sunu cynric to þam rice & heold seofan
winter.
 17. Þa he gefor.
 17. Þa feng ceolwin to þam rice & heold seofan gear.
 19. Þa he gefor.
 19. Þa feng ceol to þam rice & heold syx gear.
 20. Þa he gefor.
 21. Þa feng ceolwulf to his broþor & he ricsode seofantyne
gear & hiora cyn gæð to cerdice.
 23. Þa feng cynegils ceolwulfes broþor sunu to rice &
ricsode an & ðritti wintra & he onfeng ærest fulwihte wesseaxna
cyninga.
 26. & þa feng cenwalh to & heold an & ðritti
wintra.
 28. & se cenwald wæs cynegilses sunu & þa heold
seaxburh his cwen an gear þæt rice æfter him.
 30. Þa feng æscwine to rice þæs cynn gæð to cerdice
& heold twa gear.
 32. Þa feng centwine to wesseaxna rice cynegilsing & ricsode
seofan gear.
 34. Þa feng ceadwalla to þam rice þæs cyn gæð to
cerdice & heold twa gear.
 36. Þa feng Ine to wesseaxna rice þæs cyn gæð to
cerdice & heold syx & ðritti wintra.
 38. Þa feng æðelheard to þæs cyn gæð to cerdice
& heold feowertyne winter.
 40. Þa feng cuþred to þæs cyn gæð to cerdice &
heold seofantyne gear.
 42. Þa feng sigebyrht to þæs cyn gæð to cerdice &
heold an gear.
 44. Þa feng cynewulf to rice þæs cyn gæð to cerdice
& heold & an & ðrytti wintra.
 46. Þa feng beorhtric to rice þæs cyn gæð to cerdice
& heold syxtyne gear.
 48. Þa feng ecbyrht to þam rice & heold seofen &
ðrytti wintra & seofen monað.
 50. & þa feng æþelwulf to his sunu & heold
nigenteoðe healf gear.
 52. Se æþelwulf wæs ecbyrhting, Ecbyrht Ealhmunding,
Ealhmund Eafing, Eafa Eopping, Eoppa Ingylding, Ingyld Cenreding & Ine
Cenreding & Cuþburhg Cenreding & Cwenburhg Cenreding, Cenred
Ceolwalding, Ceolwald Cuþwulfing, Cuðwulf Cuþwining, Cuþwine Celming,
Celm Cynricing, Cynric, Cerdiccing.
 61. Ond þa feng æðelbald his sunu to rice & heold fif
ger.
 62. Þa feng æþelbyrht his broður to & heold fif ger.
 64. Þa feng æþered to heora broþor to rice & heold fif
ger.
 65. Þa feng ælfred hiora broþor to rice & þa wæs
agan his ylde twa & twenti wintra.
 67. & ðreo hund & syx & hundnigentig wintra þæs
te his cyn ærest westseaxna lond on wealum geeodon.

END_TEXT

KSB 4 (Dickins)
B18.4.
London, British Library, MS. Cotton Tiberius A.III, fol. 178: Dickins 1952, 3-5.



 1. Ða wæs agangen fram cristes acennednesse cccc & xciiii
wintra ða cerdic & cynric his sunu coman upp æt cerdices oran mid v
scipum.
 3. And se cerdic wæs elesing, Elesa esling, Esla giwising, giwis
wiging, Wig freawining, Freawine freoþogaring, Freoþogar branding, Brand
bældæging, Bældæg wodening.
 6. And þæs embe vi gear þe hie upp coman, hie geeodan
westsexna land & þæt wæron þa ærestan cingas þe
westsexnaland æt wealum genaman.
 8. And he hæfde þæt rice xvi winter.
 8. Þa gefor he & feng his sunu cynric to ðam rice, &
heold xxvi wintra.
 9. Þa he forðferde þa feng ceawlin to his sunu, & heold
xvii gear.
 10. Þa he gefor þa feng ceol to ðam rice & heold v gear.
 11. Þa he gefor ða feng ceolfwulf to his broðor, & rixode
xvii gear, & heora cynn gæð to cerdice.
 13. Þa feng cynegils to ceolwulfes broðor sunu to rice &
rixode xx wintra & he onfeng ærest fulwihte westsexna cinga.
 15. And þa feng cenwalh to & heold xxxi wintra.
 16. Se cenwealh wæs cynegilses sunu.
 16. And þa heold sexburh cwen an gear þæt rice æfter
him.
 17. Ða feng æscwine to rice.
 17. Þæs cynn gæð to cerdice & heold ii gear.
 18. Þa feng centwine to westsexna rice cinegilsing & rixode
viiii gear.
 19. Ða feng ceadwalla to þam rice.
 20. Þæs cynn gæð to cerdice & heold iii gear.
 21. Ða feng ine to westsexna rice þæs cynn gæþ to
cerdice & heold xxxvii wintra.
 22. Þa feng æþelheard to þæs cynn gæþ to cerdice
& heold xvi gear.
 23. Þa feng sigebriht to þæs cynn gæð to cerdice &
heold i gear.
 24. Þa feng cynewulf to þæs cynn gæþ to cerdice &
heold xxxi wintra.
 25. Þa feng brihtric to rice þæs cyn gæþ to cerdice
& heold xvi gear.
 26. Þa feng ecgbriht to þam rice & heold xxxvii wintra
& vii monað.
 27. Þa feng aþelwulf his sunu to & heold ix teoðe healf
gear.
 28. Se aþelwulf wæs ecgbrihting, Ecgbriht ealhmunding,
Ealhmund eafing, Eafa eopping, eoppa ingilding, ingild cenreding & ine
cenreding & cuðburh cenreding & cwenburh cenreding, Cenred
ceolwalding, Ceolwald cuþwulfing, Cuðwulf cuðwining, Cuðwine celming,
Celm cynricing, Cinric creoding, Creoda cerdicing.
 34. And þa feng æþelbald his sunu to & heold v gear.
 35. Þa feng æþelbriht his broðor to & heold v gear.
 35. Ða feng ælfred heora broðor to & heold oþran
healfan geare læs þe xxx wintra.
 37. Þa feng eadweard to.
 37. Ælfreding & heold xxiiii wintra.
 38. Ða he forðferde.
 38. Þa feng æþelstan to his sunu & heold xiiii gear
& vii wucan & iii dagas.
 39. Þa feng eadmund to his broþor & heol seofoðe healf
gear butan ii nihtum.
 40. Ða feng eadred his broþor to & heold ix gear & vi
wucan.
 41. Þa feng eadwig to.
 42. Eadmundes sunu cinges & heold iii gear & xxxvi wucena.
 43. Buton ii dagum.
 43. Þa he forðferde þa feng eadgar to his broðor &
heold xvi gear & viii wucan & ii niht.
 44. Ða he forðferde þa feng eadweard to eadgares sunu &
heold.

END_TEXT

KSB 5.2 (Wright-Halliwell)
B18.5.2.
London, British Library, MS. Cotton Tiberius B.V, vol. 1: Wright and Halliwell 1841-3, II, 172-3 (West-Saxon Genealogy).



 1. <foreign>Haec sunt genealogiae regum Occidentalium Saxonum</foreign>.
 2. Eadweard & Eadmund & Æðelred æðelingas syndon,
Eadgares suna cyninges.
 3. Eadgar Eadmunding, Eadmund Eadwerding, Eadweard Ælfreding,
Ælfred Aþolfing, Aþulf Ecgbyrhting, Ecgbriht Ealhmunding, Ealhmund
Eauing, Eaua Eopping, Eoppa Ingelding.
 6. Ingeld wæs Ines broðor Westseaxna cyninges, & he heold
rice vii & xxx wintra, & he getimbrade þæt beorhte mynster æt
Glæstingabyrig, & æfter þam fyrde to sancte Petres, & þær
his feorh asealde & on sibbe gerest, & hi begen broðra wæron
Cenredes suna.
 10. Cenred wæs Ceolwalding, Ceolwald Cuðing, Cuþa
Cuðwining, Cuðwine Ceawlining, Ceawlin Cynricing, Cynric Creoding, Creoda
Cynricing, Cerdic Elesing, Elesa Esling, Esla Gewisling, Gewis Wiging, Wig
Freawining, Freawine Freoðegaring, Freoðegar Branding, Brand
Bældæging, Bældæg Wodening, Woden Frealafing, Frealaf Finning, Finn
Godulfing, Godulf Eating, Eat Beawing, Beaw Scealdwaging, Scealwa Heremoding,
Heremod Itermanning, Iterman Haðraing, Haðra Bedwiging, Bedwig Sceafing.
 19. Se Scef wæs Noes sunu, & he wæs innan þære earce
geboren.
 20. Noe wæs Lameches sunu, Lameh Maþusalemys, Maðusalem
wæs Enoches, Enoh, Lared, Malalehel, Caino, Enos, <foreign>et</foreign> Ada, <foreign>primus homo et
pater omnium qui est Christus</foreign>.
 24. Heingils, Wealhstod, Coengils, Beorhtwald, Cealdhun, Luca,
Wiccea, Bosa, Stiðheard, Herefyrð, Hunbeorht, Andhun, Guðlac, Cuðred,
Ecgwulf, Dunstan, Ælfric, Sigegar, Ælfweard.

KSB 6 (Birch)
B18.6.
London, British Library, MS. Stowe 944: Birch 1892, 94-6.



 1. <foreign>Nomina regum</foreign>.
 1. Ine cinge rixode xxxvii wintra & on mang þam for to Rome
& þær geendode.
 2. Þa feng æfter him Æðelheard to & rixode xiiii
gear.
 4. Þa æfter him feng Cuðred to & rixode xiiii gear.
 5. Þa feng Sigebyrht to & rixode i gear.
 6. Þa feng Cynewulf to & rixode xxx wintra.
 7. Þa feng Byrhtric to cynerice & heold xvi gear.
 8. Þa feng Ecgbyrht to þam rice, & heold xxxv wintra &
vii monað.
 10. And þa feng Aðelwulf his sunu to & heold nigonteoðe
healf gear.
 12. Þa feng Aðelbald his sunu to & heold v gear.
 13. Þa feng Æðelbyrht his broðor to & rixode vi gear.
 14. Þa feng Æðered to his broðor & heold v gear.
 15. Þa feng Ælfred heora broðor to & heold oðrum
healfan geare læsse þonne xxx wintra.
 17. Þa feng Eadweard to Ælfredes sunu & heold xxiiii
wintra þa he forðferde.
 19. Þa feng Æþelstan to his sunu & heold xiiii gear
& vii wucan & iii dagas.
 21. Þa feng Eadmund to his broðor & heold seofoðe healf
gear butan twam nihtum.
 23. Þa feng Eadred to his broþor & heold viiii gear &
vi wucan.
 25. Þa feng Eadwig to Eadmundes sunu cingces & heold iii gear
& xxxvi wucena butan twam dagum þa he forðferde.
 28. Þa feng Eadgar to his broðor & heold xvi gear &
viii wucan.
 30. Þa feng Eadweard to Eadgares sunu & heold iiii gear butan
xvi wucan þa he forðferde.
 32. Þa feng Æþelred to rice his broðor & he rixode
xxxviii geara.
 34. Þa feng Cnut cingc to rice.

KSB 7.1 (Ingram)
B18.7.1.
Rochester, Cathedral, Textus Roffensis: Ingram 1823, 375-6.



 1. Ða wæs agangen fram cristes accennednesse cccc and xciiii
wintra ða Cerdic and Cynric his sunn coman up æt Cerdius oran mid v
scipum.
 3. And se Cerdic wæs elesing, Eles gewising, Gewis wiging, Wig
freawining, Freawine Freoðogaring, Freoðegar branding, Brond
bældæging, Bældæg wodening.
 6. Þæs ymb vi gear þæs ðe hy up comon hi geeodan west
seaxana rice, and þæt wæron þa ærestan cynegas ðe west seaxana
land on wealum geodon.
 9. And he hæfde þæt rice xvi gear.
 9. Þa he gefor, þa feng Cynric his suno to þam rice, and
heold xxvi wintra.
 10. Þa he forðferde.
 11. Þa feng Ceaulin his sunu to, and heold vii gear, þa he
gefor.
 12. Þa feng Ceol to, and heold vi gear.
 12. Ða he gefor, þa feng Ceolulf to his broðor, and he
ricsode xvii gear.
 14. Heora cyn gæð to Cerdice.
 14. Ða feng Cynegils Ceolwulfes broðor sunu to ðam rice, and
heold xxxi wintra.
 16. And he onfeng ærest fulluht west seaxana cyninga.
 17. And þa feng Cenwealh to and heold xxxi wintra, and se
Cenwealh wæs Cynegilses sunu.
 18. And þa heold Sexburh his cwen an gear þæt rice æfter
him.
 19. Ða feng Æscwine to ðam rice, ðæs cyn gæð to
Cerdice, and he heold ii gear.
 21. Ða feng Centwine cynegilsing to westseaxan rice, and ricsode
ix gear.
 22. Ða feng Cedwalla to, ðæs cyn gæð to Cerdice, and
heold iii gear.
 23. Ða feng Ine to West sexena rice, ðæt cyn gæð to
Cerdice, and heold xxxvii wintra.
 25. Ða feng Æðelheard to, ðæs cyn gæð to Cerdice,
and heold xiiii gear.
 26. Ða feng Cuðred to, ðes cyn gæð to Cerdice, and heold
xvi gear.
 27. Ða feng Sigebirht to, ðæs cyn gæð to Cerdice, and
heold i gear.
 28. Ða feng Cynwulf to ðam rice, ðæs cyn gæð to
Cerdice, and heold xxxi wintra.
 30. Ða feng Beorhtric to ðam rice, ðæs cyn gæð to
Cerdice, and heold xvi gear.
 31. Ða Ecgbyrht feng to ðam rice and heold xxxvii wintra and
vii monað.
 32. Ða feng Aðulf his sunu to þam rice, and heold teoðe
healf gear.
 33. Se Aðulf wæs ecgbyrhting, Ecgbriht ealhmunding, Ealhmund
eabing, Eaba eopping, Ioppa ingylding, Ingild cenreding, and Ine cenreding, and
Cuðburh cenreding, and Cwenburh cenreding, Cenred ceolwalding, Ceolwald
cuðwulfing Cuðwulf cuðwinning, Cuðwine celining, Celin cynricing,
Cynric creoding, Creoda Cerdicing.
 39. Æfter Aðulfe feng Æthelbald his sunu to ðam rice, and
heold v gear.
 41. Þa feng Æþelbyrht and heold v gear, After him
Æðelred v gear.
 42. Ða feng Ælfred to westseaxana rice, and heold xxviii healf
gear.
 43. Hy ealle feower wæron Aðulfes suna, Æðelbald,
Æðelbriht, Æðelred and Ælfred.
 45. After Ælfrede feng Eadward his sunu to ðam rice and heold
xxiiii wintra.
 46. Ða feng Ælfwerd Eadwardes sunu to, and heold iiii wucan.
 47. Ða feng Æþelstan his broðor to, and wiglice þæs
rices weold.
 48. His timan ealne þæt wæs xiiii gear and x wucan.
 49. Ða feng Eadmund his broðor to ðam rice, and heold
seofoðe healf gear.
 50. Ða feng Eadred to and heold teoðe healf gear.
 51. After Ædrede feng Eadwig Eadmundes sunu to ðam rice and
heold ðridde healf gear.
 52. Ða feng Eadgear to, and mid wislican wære ðæs rices
weold xvi gear and viii wucan.
 54. After him feng Eadwerd his sunu to and heold iii gear &
eahta monþe.
 55. Ða feng Æðelred to and þæs rices weold xxxviii
gear.
 56. Æðelred wæs Eadgaring, Eadgar Eadmunding.
 56. Eadmund Eadweording, Eadweard Ælfreding, Ælfred
Aðulfing, Aðulf Ecgbyrhting, Ecgbyrht ealhmunding, Ealhmund eabing Eaba
eopping, Ioppa ingilding, Ingild cenreding, Cenred ceolwalding, Ceolwald
cuðulfing, Cuðulf cuðwining, Cuðwine celining, Celin cinricing, Cinric
creoding, Creoda cerdicing.
 62. Se Cerdic wæs swa ic ær cwæþ se forma þe west
sexana land mid wige on wealum geeode, and his ofspryncg dyde swa him gebyrde
wæs fæste bewerode þæt he ærost gewann.
 65. Eac eacan begeat heora anra gewelhwilc symle be ðam cræfte
þe heom God lænde.

END_TEXT
START_TEXT

KSB 7.2 (Hearne)
B18.7.2.
Rochester, Cathedral, Textus Roffensis: Hearne 1720, 59-60 (Anglian Genealogy).



 1. Ðisys Angel Cynnes Cyne Cynn þe her gemearcod is.
 2. Adam þæs se æresta man, & he gestrinde Seth.
 3. And Seth gestrinde Enos.
 3. And Enos gestrinde Kainan.
 4. And Kainan gestrinde Malaleel.
 4. And Maleel gestrinde Iared.
 5. And Iared gestrinde Enoch.
 6. Æfter Enoch wæs Matusalam.
 6. Þa wæs Lamech.
 6. Þa wæs Noe.
 7. Þa wæs Sem.
 7. Þa wæs Scyf, se wæs in tham arken geboran.
 9. Ða wæs Bedwig.
 9. Ða wæs Hwala.
 9. Ða wæs Haþra.
 9. Ða wæs Iterman.
 10. Ða wæs Heremod.
 10. Ða wæs Sealdra.
 10. Ða wæs Beaw.
 11. Ða wæs Tethuua.
 11. Ða wæs Geata.
 11. Ðe ne ða hæþena wurþedon for god.
 13. Ða wæs Godwulf.
 13. Ða wæs Finn.
 13. Ða wæs Friðewulf.

KSB 8.1 (Liebermann)
B18.8.1.
Cambridge, Corpus Christi College, MS. 201: Liebermann 1889, 1-9 (English Kings).



 1. Her cyð ymbe þa halgan þe on Angelcynne restað, on ures
Drihtenes naman, hælendes Cristes.
 2. Sanctus Agustinus gefullode Æþelbriht Cantwarena cyningc
and ealle his þeode.
 3. Ðonne wæs Eadbald Æþelbrihtes sunu cynges, and
Birihtan hatte his cwen.
 4. And Æþelburh hatte heora dohtor and oðre naman Tate, heo
wæs forgifen Eadwine Norðhymbra cyninge to cwene, and sanctus Paulinus, se
mæra biscop, for mid hire and gefullode þone cyning and ealle his
þeode.
 5. And heo þa æfter Eadwines dæge gesohte Cantwarabirig,
and hire broðor Eadbald wæs Cantwara cyningc, and he hire þa forgeaf
þæt land on Limene, and heo þa þæt mynster getymbrode, and þar nu
resteð, and sancta Eadburh mid hyre.
 6. Ðonne wæs Ymme, Eadbaldes cwen, Franca cynges dohtor, and
hig begeaton sancte Eanswiðe, þe æt Folcanstane restað, and
Earcanbriht Cantwara cyningc and Eormenred æþelingc.
 7. And Eormenburh and sancte Eormengið and sancte Æþelred
and sancte Æþelbriht þis wæron Eormenrædes bearn and Oslafe, his
cwene.
 8. Ðonne wæs Ecgbriht cyningc and Loðhere cyningc and sancta
Eormenhild and sancta Ercengota wæron Ercenbrihtes bearn and Sexburge, his
cwene.
 9. Þonne wæs sancte Eormenburge oðer nama Domne Eue, heo
wæs forgifen Merwale, Pendan sunu cynges, and þar hi begeaton sancte
Mildburge and sancte Mildryþe and sancte Mildgiðe and sancte Merefynn.
 10. Hi þa for Godes lufan todældon be heom libbendum hi
gedældon be him lybbendan eal þæt hi ahton; and heo þa Domne Eue for
eft to Cæntlande and hyre broðra wergildes onfengc innon Tænetlande
æt Ecgbrihte þam cyninge, þe hig ær acwellan het.
 11. Ðunor hatte his gerefa, þe hig acwellan het, and he hig
bebirigde under þæs cynges heahsetle on Eastrege innon his healle, and hi
þa wurdon þurh Godes naman wundorlice gecydde, swa þæt þurh Godes
mihte se leoma astod ymbe midderniht up þurh þare healle hrof, swilce þar
sunne scine; and þæt se cyningc him silf geseah, and he wæs swiðe
afyrht and he þa be þam wiste, þæt he hæfde þam hælende
abolgen.
 12. And he þa het heora swustor Domne Eue him to gefeccan,
þæt heo heora wergilde onfon mihte and heo þa swa dyde, þæt is
þonne hundeahtati sulunga landes, þæt hig þæt mynster on
arærdon, þam sawlum to gebedrædenne, þe hit heora wergild wæs, and
se cyningc hire þarto wel filste.
 13. And heo þa sancte Mildriðe, hire dohtor, ofer sæ
sænde, þæt heo þone wisdom þar geleornode, þe man on þam
mynstre healdan scolde, and heo þa swa dide and þar micelne haligdom
begeat, þe man nu git to dæg þær sceawian mæg.
 14. And heo þa, sancte Mildryð, eft to hyre medder ham com, and
heo hire þa þæt mynster forgeaf, þa hit gestaðelod wæs, and heo
þa, sancte Mildryð, halig rifte onfengc æt Theodore arcebiscope, and
hundseofontig mædena mid hyre, þe se cyningc and hire modor begiten
hæfdon and gelæred, þæt hig æt þare stowe nytte beon mihton.
 15. And heo þa þar Gode to willan geþeah and þæt ece lif
geearnode, and swa oft siððan heora mihta cuðe syndon.
 16. And sancte Eormengið, hyre moddrige, mid hire wunode oð
hire lifes ende and heo silf þar hyre licreste geceas be hire libbendre,
þæt is þonne an mil be easton sancte Myldryðe mynstre, and hyre mihta
þar oft wæron cuðe and git syndon.
 17. And sancte Eadburh þa to þam mynstre fengc æfter sancte
Myldriðe and heo þa circan gesette, þe heora lichama nu on resteð.
 18. Ðonne wæs Sexburh Cantwarena cwen, heo gestaðelode
sancta Marian mynster on Sceapege and þa Godes þeowas þarto gesette,
hwæt, þa Loðhere cyningc, hyre sunu, heom þare landare geuþe, þe
hig git big libbað, and heo þa gebedrædene þar arærdon.
 19. Ðonne wæs sancte Sexburh and sancta Æþeldryð and
sancta Wihtburh Annan dohtra Eastengla cyninges.
 20. Ðonne wæs sancte Æþeldryð forgifen Ecgfryðe
Norðhymbra cynge to cwene, and heo hwæðre hyre mægðhad geheold oð
hyre lifes ende, and heo þa hire licreste geceas on Eligabirig, on þam
mæran mynstre, and þar hyre mihta oft cuðe syndon.
 21. And sancta Wihtburh, hire swustor, mid hire nu restað.
 22. Ðonne wæs sancta Eormenhild, Ercenbrihtes dohtor and
Sexburge, forgifen Wulfhere cyninge to cwene; he wæs Pendan sunu Myrcna
cynges.
 23. And on heora dagum Myrcna þeod onfeng fulwihte.
 24. And ðar hi begeaton sancta Wærburge, þa halgan
fæmnan, and heo wearð bebirged on þam mynstre þe is genemnod Heanburh,
heo wearð eft upadon and nu resteð on Legeceastre þare birig.
 25. Ðonne resteð sancte Eormenhild on Eligabirig mid hyre
medder and mid hyre moddrian sancte Æþeldryðe, and hyre mihta þar oft
cuðe syndon.
 26. Ðonne wæs sancte Ercengota heora swustor gesænd ofer
sæ to lare to hire moddrian sancte Æþelburge, ðar heo wæs
abbodesse, and heo þar Gode to willan geþeah and þar hire lif geendode,
and hire mihta þar sona cuðe wæron.
 27. Ðonne wæs Wihtred cyningc Ecgbrihtes sunu cyninges, and he
arærde þæt mynster on Doferan and hit gehalgode sancte Martine to
wurðunge, and sanctus Martinus him silf ær þa stowe getacnode, þæt
he his mynster þar habban wolde, and he þa swa dyde and þa Godes þeowas
þarto gesette mid þare landare, þe he heom þarto geuðe, þe hig git
big libbað oð þisne andweardan dæg.
 28. And he resteð hine æt Sancte Agustine innon þam portice
on suðhealfe sancta Marian circan, þe his þridda fæder Eadbold cyningc
het asettan Gode to lofe and sancta Marian.

KSB 10.1 (Birch)
B18.10.1.
London, British Library, MS. Stowe 944: Birch 1892, 83-7 (English Saints).



 1. Her cyð ymbe þa halgan þe on angel cynne restað.
 2. On ures drihtnes naman hælendes Cristes, Sanctus Augustinus
gefullode æþelbyrht Cantwara cyningc & ealle his þeode.
 4. Þonne wæs Eadbald æðelbyrhtes sunu cyninges, &
Byrhtan hatte his cwen, & æðelburh hatte heora dohtor, oþrum naman
Tate.
 6. Heo wæs forgyfen Eadwine Norðhymbra cyninge to cwene, &
Sanctus Paulinus se bisceop for mid hyre & gefullode þone cyningc, &
ealle his þeode.
 9. And heo þa eft æfter Eadwines dæge gesohte Cantwara
byrig.
 10. And hyre broðor Eadbald, wæs þa Cantwara cyningc.
 11. And he hyre þa forgeaf þæt land on Limmingce & heo
þa þæt mynster getimbrade & þær nu resteð, & sancta
Eadburh mid hyre.
 14. Þonne wæs Imme Eadbaldes cwen Francena cyningces dohtor,
& hi begeaton Sancte Eanswiðe þe æt Folcanstane resteð, &
Earcanbyrht Cantwara cyningc, & Eormenræd æþelingc, &
Eormenbeorgan, & sancte Eormenburge, & sancte Eormengyde, & sancte
æþelred, & sancte æþelbyrht.
 19. Þis wæron Eormenrædes bearn & Oslaue.
 20. Þonne wæs Ecgbyrht cyningc, & Loðhere cyningc, &
sancta Eormenhild, & sancta Ercengota wæron Eorcenbyrhtes bearn, &
Sexburge his cwene.
 23. Þonne wæs sancte Eormenbeorge oðer naman Domne Eue, heo
wæs forgyfen Merwale Penda sunu cyningces, & þær hi begeaton Sancte
Mildburge, & sancte Mildryðe, & sancte Mildgyðe, & sancte
Merefin.
 27. Hi þa for Godes lufon hi gedældon be him lybbendan, &
heo þa Domne Eue for eft to Centlande.
 28. And hyre broðra wergildes onfengc binnan Tenetlande æt
Ecgbyrhte þam cyningce þe hi ær acwellan het.
 30. Þunor hatte his gereua þe hi acwellan het, & he hi
bebyrigde under þæs cyningces heahsetle on Eastrege innan his healle.
 33. And hi þa wurdon þurh Godes naman gecydde swa þæt
þurh Godes mihte se leoma stod ymbe midde niht up þurh þære healle
hrof swylce þær sunne scine, & þæt se cyningc him sylf geseah.
 36. And he wæs swiðe afyrht, & he þa be þam wiste
þæt he hæfde Gode abolgen, & he þa het heora swustor Domne Euan
him to gefeccean þæt heo heora wergyld on fon mihte.
 39. And heo þa swa dyde, þæt is þonne LXXX sulunga landes,
þæt hi þæt mynster on arærdon þam sawlum to gebedrædenne þe
hit heora wergyld wæs.
 42. And se Ecgbyrht hyre þær to wel gefylste.
 43. And heo þa sancte Mildryðe hire dohtor ofer sæ sende,
þæt heo þonne wisdom þær geleornode þe man on þam mynstre
healdan sceolde.
 45. And heo þa swa dyde, & þær micelne haligdom beget
þe mon nu gyt to dæg sceawian mæg.
 47. And heo þa sancte Mildryð eft to hyre meder ham com &
heo hyre þa þæt mynster forgeaf þa hit gestaðolad wæs.
 49. And heo þa sancta Mildryð haligryfte onfengc æt Theodore
arcebisceope, & LXX mædena mid hyre þe se cyningc & hyre modor
begyten hæfdon & gelæred þæt hi æt þære stowe nytte beon
mihton.
 53. And heo þa þær Gode to willan geþeah, & þæt
ece lif geearnode.
 54. And swa oft syððan heora mihta cuðe syndon, & sancte
Ermengyð hyre moddrie mid hyre wunode oð hyre lifes ende.
 56. And heo sylf þær hyre lic reste geceas be hyre lybbendre,
þæt is þonne an mil be eastan Sancte Mildryðe mynstre, & hyre
mihta þær oft wæron & gyt a cuðe synd.
 59. And Sancte Eadburh þa to þam mynstre feng æfter sancte
Mildryðe, & heo þa cyricean gesette þe hyre lichama nu on resteð.
 62. Þonne wæs Sexburh Cantwara cwen.
 62. Heo gestaðolade Sancta Marian mynster on Sceapige, & þa
Godes þeowas þær to gesette.
 64. And þa Loðhere cyningc hyre sunu him þære land are
geuðe þe hi gyt big lybbað & heora gebedrædenne þær
arædon.
 67. Þonne wæs sancta Sexburh, & sancte æðeldryþ,
& sancta þihtburh, Annan dohtra east Engla cingces.
 69. Þonne wæs sancta æþeldryð forgyfen Ecgfriðe
Norðhymbra cyningce to cwene.
 70. And heo hræðere hyre mægðhad geheold oð hyre lifes
ende.
 71. And heo þa hyre lic reste geceas on Eliga byrig on þam
mæran mynstre, & þær hyra mihta oft cuðe syndon.
 73. And sancta Wihtburh hyre sweostor mid hyre nu þær
resteð.
 74. Þonne wæs sancta Eormenhild Ercenbyrhtes dohtor &
Sexburge forgyfen Wulfhere cyningce to cwene.
 76. He wæs Pendan sunu Myrcna cyningces.
 77. And on heora dagum Myrcna þeod onfengc fulluhte, &
þær hi begeaton sancte þærburge þa halgan fæmnan.
 79. And heo wæs bebyriged on þam mynstre þe is genemned Hean
burh, & nu resteð on Legceastre þære byrig.
 82. Þonne resteð Sancte Eormenhyld on Eliga byrig mid hyre
meder & mid hyre moddrian sancte æðeldryþe, & hyre mihta
þær oft cuðe syndon.
 84. Þonne wæs Sancta Ercengota heora sweostor gesend ofer
sæ to lare to hyre moddrian Sancte æþelburge þær heo wæs
abbodysse.
 87. And heo þær Gode to willan geþeah, & þær hyre
lif geendode.
 88. And hyre mihta þær cuðe sona wæron.
 88. Þonne wæs Wihtred cyningc Ecgbyrhtes sunu cyningces, &
he arærde þæt mynster on Doferum & hit gehalgode Sancte Martine to
wurðunge.
 91. And Sanctus Martinus him sylf ær þa stowe getacnode
þæt he his mynster þær habban wolde, & he þa swa dyde.
 93. And þa Godes þeowas þær to gesette mid þære
landare þe he him þær to geuðe þe hi gyt big lybbað oð þysne
dæg.
 95. And he resteð hine æt Sancte Augustine innan þam portice
on suð healfe Sancta Marian cyricean, þe his þridda fæder Eadbold
cyningc het asettan Gode to lofe & Sancta Marian.

END_TEXT

KSB 10.2 (Birch)
B18.10.2.
London, British Library, Stowe 944: Birch 1892, 87-94 (English Saints).



 1. Her ongynð secgean be þam Godes sanctum þe on Engla lande
ærest reston.
 2. Sanctus Albanus martyr in Breotone se resteð neah Wælinga
ceastre he þære ea þe is genemned Wærlame.
 3. Þonne resteð Columcylle on þære stowe þe is genemned
Duncabeam neah þære ea þe is genemned Tau.
 4. Þonne resteð Sanctus Cuðberhtus on þære stowe seo is
genemned Ubban ford neh þære ea þe is genemned Twiode.
 5. Þonne resteð Sancta Oswald cyningc on Bebban byrig wið
þa sæ, & his heafod resteð mid sancte Guðberhte, & his
swyðra earm is nu on Bebban byrig, & his lichama resteð nu on niwan
mynstre on Gleaw ceastre.
 6. Þonne resteð Sanctus Johannes on þære stowe Beferlic
neh þære ea Hull.
 7. Þonne resteð sancte Ecgbyrht, & sancte Wilferð
bisceop, & sancte Wihtburht, on þam mynstre þe is genemned æt
Hryopan neh þære ea þe hatte Earp.
 8. Þonne resteð sancte Ceadda, & sancte Cedde, & sancte
Ceatta on þam mynstre þe is genemned Licetfeld, neh þære ea þe is
gehaten Tame.
 9. Þonne resteð sancte Higebold on Lindisse, on þære stowe
þe is genemned Cecesegi, neh þære ea þe is genemned on Cel.
 10. Þonne resteð Sancte Æðered se cyningc on þam mynstre
þe is genemned Bardanig neh þære ea þe is gehaten Wiðma.
 11. Þonne resteð Sancte Eadburh on þam mynstre æt
Suðwyllum neh þære ea þe is genemned Treonte.
 12. Þonne resteð sancte Guðlac on þære stowe þe is
genemned Cruland, þæt mynster is on middan Gyrwan fenne.
 13. Þonne resteð Sancte Ealhmund on þam mynstre
Norðweorðig neah þære ea Deorwentan.
 14. Þonne wæs sancte Botolf gebyrged on þam mynstre þe is
genemned Medes hamstede, þæt is neahburh þære ea Nen.
 15. Þonne resteð sancte Æðelbyrht æt þam bisceopstole
æt Hereforda neah þære ea Wæge.
 16. Þonne resteð Sancte Cett on þam mynstre þe is genemned
Undola, neah þære ea Nen.
 17. Þonne resteð Sancte Mildburh on þam mynstre Wynlocan neah
þære ea þe mon Sæfern hateð.
 18. Þonne resteð Sancte Wigstan on þam mynstre Hreopedune,
neah þære ea Treante.
 19. Þonne resteð Sancte Dioma on þære stowe þe is
genemned Ceorlingburh, neah þære ea Wenrisc.
 20. Þonne resteð Sancta Eadgyð on þære stowe þe is ge
haten Polles wyrð neah þære ea Oncer.
 21. Þonne resteð Sancte Rumwald on þære stowe þe is
gehaten Buccingaham, neah þære ea Usan.
 22. Þonne resteð Sancte Æþelbyrht on þam mynstre þe
man hateð Bydanford, neah þære ea Usan.
 23. Þonne resteð Sancte Æþelred æt Leo mynster neah
þære ea Lucge.

 25. Þonne resteð Sancta Osgyð oc Cicc neah þære sæ on

 26. Þonne resteð Sancta Æþelburh on þam mynstre æt
Beorcingan neah Temese.
 27. Þonne resteð sancte Ercenwald bisceop on Lunden byrig.
 28. Þonne resteð Sancte Neot mæsse preost on Eanulfes
byrig.
 29. Þonne restað æt Hramesige Sancte Iua, & Sancte
Æþelred & sancte Æþelbyrht.
 30. Þonne restað on Burh Sanctus Florentius martyr, &
sancta Cyneswið, & sancta Cyneburh, & monige oðre þeah hi mannum
digle syn, for þam ne wyrcað ealle halige mann wundra.
 31. Þonne restað on þornige Sancte Botulf, & sancte
Aþulf, & sancte Huna, & sancte þancred, & sancte Torhtred,

 32. Þonne resteð on Abbadune Sanctus Uincentius martyr.
 33. Þonne resteð Sanctus Dunstanus arcebisceop, on Cantwara

 34. Þonne resteð Sanctus Paulinus on Hrofe ceastre.

 36. Þonne restað on niwan mynstre Sanctus Iudocus, &
Sanctus Grimbaldus.

& fela oðra haligra bisceopa mid him.

 40. Þonne resteð sancte Kenelm cynebearn on Winclescumbe.

& Iohann se wisa on Ealdelmes byrig.
 42. Þonne resteð Sancte Iwig & sancta Eadgyð on Wiltune.

 44. Þonne resteþ sanctus Aidanus, & sanctus Patricius on

 47. Þonne Rumonus episcopus on Tæfistoce.
 48. Þonne resteð sanctus Petrocus on west Wealum be þære

 49. Þonne resteþ sancte Cuðburh on Winburnan mynstre, þe

 50. Þonne resteð sancta Frideswyð on Oxnaforda.

Suðsexum neah þære ea Bremre.

Mart 1 (Herzfeld-Kotzor)
B19.1.
Cambridge, Corpus Christi College, MS. 41: Herzfeld 1900, 2-10; corrected by Kotzor, 1981.



 2. <foreign>DE25A/1</foreign> On þone forman dæig on geare, þæt is on
þone ærestan geoheldæig, eall cristen folc worþiað Cristes
acennednesse.
 3. <foreign>DE25A/3</foreign> Sancta Maria hine acende on þære nihte on anum
holum stanscræfe beforan Bethem ðære ceastre, ond sona ða he acenned
wæs, heofonlic leoht scean ofer eall þæt land, ond godes engel
ætiwde sceeaphirdon on anre mile be eastan þære cestre.
 7. <foreign>DE25A/8</foreign> And him sæde þæt eallra folca hælend
wære acenned, ond ða hirdas gehirdon micelne engla sang on eorðan.
 9. <foreign>DE25A/10</foreign> Þa wæs agangen fram middangeardes fruman fif
þusend geare ond ane geare læs þonne twa hund þa Crist was acenned.
 11. <foreign>DE25A/13</foreign> On þam geare þa he wæs acenned þa
æteowdon swilc tacn mannum swilce ær næron ne næfre siðan.
 13. <foreign>DE25A/16</foreign> Þy geare men gesawon III sunnan, ond oþre
siðe III monan.
 14. <foreign>DE25A/17</foreign> Ond Romanan gesawon firen cleowen feallan of
heofnum, ond oþre siþe gilden cleowen.
 15. <foreign>DE25A/19</foreign> Ond þi geare man geseah hwætes eare weaxan on
treowum.
 16. <foreign>DE25A/20</foreign> Ond on sumere mæigðe þonne hi hira hlaf
bræcon æt mete, þonne fleow þæt blod of þam hlafe, swa of mannes
lichaman deð þonne he gewundod bið.
 19. <foreign>DE25A/23</foreign> Ond þi geare man geseah meoloc rinan of heofnum
ond lamb spæcan on mennisc gecinde mid Egiptum ond oxa spæc on Rome to
þam ergendum.
 21. <foreign>DE25A/25</foreign> Ond he cwæð, Tohwon sticast þu me?
 21. <foreign>DE25A/27</foreign> God hwæte geweaxeð togeare.
 22. <foreign>DE25A/29</foreign> Ac ne bist ðu þonne, ne his ne abitest.
 22. <foreign>DE25A/30</foreign> Eall þis tacnode þæt seo clæne fæmne
cende sunu, swa hire næfre wer ne gehran, ac se ðe hæfde fæder on
heofnum butan meder and hæfde þa modur on eorðan butan fæder.
 25. <foreign>DE25A/34</foreign> Þæt bæð þæt sancta Maria þæt
cild on baþode þurh þæt manige untrume men þær on wurdon
gehælede.
 28. <foreign>DE25B/1</foreign> On þone ilcan dæig Cristes acennednesse godes
circean arworðiað sancta Anastasiam gebird þære halegan gesiðwifes,
seo wæs swiðe æþele for worulde ond micele betere for gode.
 30. <foreign>DE25B/4</foreign> Diocletianus se hæþena casere hi sealde his
gereuas þæt hi sceolde mid witum bregean, þæt heo Criste wiðsoce
ond hæþengild gulde.
 33. <foreign>DE25B/7</foreign> Þa het se gerefa hi belucan in carcerne sixtig
daga ond nihta, ond hire man ne sealde ne hlaf ne wæter ne nanne eorðlicne
mete.
 35. <foreign>DE25B/10</foreign> Hire com ælce niht sumes haliges wifes gast to,
seo wæs haten sancta Theodote, ond broht hire heofonlicu gereordu, ond
sæde hire be þære heofonlican fægernesse, ond wunode mid hire oð
hanasang, ond eft ferde to heofonum.
 38. <foreign>DE25B/15</foreign> Ða æfter syxtigum dagum, þa heo ut eode of
þam carcerne, þa wæs hire ansin swa reod ond swa fæiger swa
þære winsumestan fæmnan, þonne heo fægerost bið.
 41. <foreign>DE25B/18</foreign> Þurh wuldorlicne martyrdom heo forlet þis
andwearde lif, ond hire lichama resteð nu on Romebirig.
 43. <foreign>DE25C/1</foreign> On ðone forman dæig bið sancta Eufemian tid
þære æþelan fæmnan.
 44. <foreign>DE25C/2</foreign> Seo wæs on Commodes dagon þæs caseres, ond
heo lufode Crist, ær heo gefullod wære.
 45. <foreign>DE25C/4</foreign> Heo wæs swiðe mæres weres dohtur, se wæs
haten Philippus.
 46. <foreign>DE25C/5</foreign> He was þære mæran burge gereua þe hatte
Alexandria, ond ealle Egipta þeode him hirdon.
 47. <foreign>DE25C/7</foreign> Þa þæt mæden wæs XV gear, þa wolde se
fæder hi sellan sumum æþelon men to bryde.
 49. <foreign>DE25C/9</foreign> Þa on niht bescear heo hire feax swa weras ond
onfeng weres gegyrlan ond gewat of hire fæder rice mid twam cnihton.
 51. <foreign>DE25C/11</foreign> Þa eode heo on wera minster, þer nan wifman
ær ne com, ond heo onfeng fulwihte ond gode þenode ond þeowode ond mid
þam wunode, þæt nan man ne mihte onfindan, þæt heo wæs
fæmne.
 54. <foreign>DE25C/15</foreign> Ond binnan III gearum heo wearð þæs minstres
abbud.
 55. <foreign>DE25C/16</foreign> Ond heo was swa mihtegu wið god þæt heo
sealde blindum men gesihðe ond deofulseoce gehælde.
 56. <foreign>DE25C/19</foreign> Ond þa æfter manegum gearum heo wæs fram
hire fæder ongitenu ond broþrum, ond siððan heo wunode mid fæmnum
on hira hiwe, ond æfter hire fæder heo gewat mid hire meder to Rome, ond
þær geþrowode martirdom for Criste.
 60. <foreign>DE25C/21</foreign> Þær Necittius, Romeburge gereua, hi nidde
þæt heo Criste wiðsoce ond deofulgild gelifde.
 61. <foreign>DE25C/23</foreign> Þa heo þæt nolde, þa het he bindan hire
stan to þam swuran ond worpan on Tifre flod.
 62. <foreign>DE25C/25</foreign> Þa tobærs se stan, ond heo fleat ofer þæt
wæter to lande.
 63. <foreign>DE25C/27</foreign> Ond þa het he hi eft sendan on birnendne ofon,
ond se acolode sona.
 64. <foreign>DE25C/29</foreign> Þa het hie don on carcern, ond heo wæs
þær X niht and dagas butan mete.
 66. <foreign>DE25C/30</foreign> Þa æteowde hire drihten silfa on þa ilcan
niht æt his acennisse ond cwæð to hire.
 67. <foreign>DE25C/32</foreign> Ic þe nime Eugenie, ond ic eom se þe þu
lufodest.
 68. <foreign>DE25C/35</foreign> Þi illcan dæge ic to heofnum astah þe þe
ic to eorþan com.
 69. <foreign>DE25C/36</foreign> Ond þi ilcan dæig heo onsende hire gast to
gode, ond hire lichama resteð wið Romebirig on þam wege þe man
nemneð Latina.
 72. <foreign>DE26A/1</foreign> On þone æfteran dæig godes circean
arworðiað sanctus Stefanus gemind þæs ærestan diacones ond þæs
ærestan martires æfter Cristes þrowunge.
 74. <foreign>DE26A/4</foreign> Þone halgan Stefanus Cristes þegnas gehalgodon
to diacone, ac Iudeas hine eft mið stanum ofwurpon, for þan þe he mid
micelre baldnisse ciðde þæt se hælend wære soð godes sunu, se
ðe hi on rode onhengon.
 77. <foreign>DE26A/8</foreign> Ond þa hi Stefanus to þære stæninge
læddon, þa mihte he locian on heofnas, ond he geseah þone hælend
silfne standan on his godþrimme.
 79. <foreign>DE26A/11</foreign> Ond he hit þam Iudeum sæde, ond hi him micle

 81. <foreign>DE26A/13</foreign> Þa leton hi his lichaman licgan butan Hierusalem

 83. <foreign>DE26A/17</foreign> Þa bebirigde hine sum geleafful man, se wæs

 84. <foreign>DE26A/20</foreign> Ond þa æfter manegum gearum wæs se lichama

untrume man þær his hælo onfeng þa hine man of eorþan updide ond
miclon lofsange læddon to Hierusalem.
 87. <foreign>DE26A/21</foreign> Þæt wæs sanctus Stefnanus wundra sum

 89. <foreign>DE26A/23</foreign> Þa nam þæs cild modor þone deadan lichaman
ond wearp on sanctus Stefanus circean þær his reliquia sum dæl inne
wæs.
 91. <foreign>DE26A/26</foreign> Þa heo eft com, þa mitte heo hire cild lifiende
ond gesund.
 93. <foreign>DE27A/1</foreign> On þone III dæig bið Sancte Iohannes tid
þæs godspellres, se wæs Criste leof ofer ealle oþre men þe he on

hlenode on þæs hælendes bearme ond ofer his breost, ond he aweahte men
of deaþe ond he gesenode II birþena gyrda, ond hie wurdan sona to þam
golde þe man hateð <foreign>abritsum</foreign>, þæt is smæte gold.
 98. <foreign>DE27A/3</foreign> Ond II beorgas litelra stana he gesenode to
æþelum gymmum.
 100. <foreign>DE27A/5</foreign> And rice hæþene men hine snidon þæt he
dranc ator, on þam was ælces cynnes wirm oððe ban oððe blod, ond
ne ablacode he.
 101. <foreign>DE27A/8</foreign> Ond his birgen is mid Grecum on Effessio þære
ceastre.
 102. <foreign>DE27A/10</foreign> Æt þære gyrgine bið wellmicel wundor

 103. <foreign>DE27A/12</foreign> Hwilon heo eðað swa lifiende man slape, hwilon
þonne man þa byrgine sceawað, þonne ne bið þær nan lichoma
gesewen, ac bið micel swetnisse stenc.
 106. <foreign>DE27A/18</foreign> Forþam nat nænig man hwæþer se Johannes
si þe cwicu þe dead.
 108. <foreign>DE28A/1</foreign> On þone feorþan dæig bið þara haligra

eald cild, forþan þe he wolde Crist acwellan on þæra cilda gemange.
 111. <foreign>DE28A/6</foreign> Herodes het tion ða cild of hira modor breostum
ond bosmum, ond þonne man þa cild cwalde, þonne spiwon hi þa meoloc
ær þæt blod.
 113. <foreign>DE28A/9</foreign> Þa wæron þa cild mid hira blode gefullode
ond þa modor mid þam tearum gefullode for þam sare þe æt þam

 116. <foreign>DE28A/11</foreign> Þæra cildea wæs tu CC and XI and IIII

 116. <foreign>DE28A/12</foreign> Ond Erodes forwearð æfter þæra cilda

 119. <foreign>DE31A/1</foreign> On þone VII dæg þæs monþes bið
<foreign>sancte</foreign> Siluestres tid þæs halgan papan, þæs lichoma resteð on

 120. <foreign>DE31A/3</foreign> Se dide fela wundra ær he papa wære.
 121. <foreign>DE31A/4</foreign> Tarquinius hatte Romeburge gereua.
 122. <foreign>DE31A/5</foreign> He þreatode hine to hæþenscipe.
 122. <foreign>DE31A/5</foreign> Þa nolde he þæt.

Mart 2.1 (Herzfeld-Kotzor)
B19.2.1.
Cambridge, Corpus Christi College, MS. 196: Herzfeld 1900, 40-222; corrected by Kotzor, 1981.



 2. <foreign>JU24A/11</foreign> he com beforan Criste on middangeard, swa se
morgensteorra cymð beforan þære sunnan, swa swa bydel beforan deman
cymð, ond swa swa byme clypað beforan cyninge.
 5. <foreign>JU24A/15</foreign> Johannes wæs se engel se ðe eode beforan gode,
forþan ðe god wolde þa forðgangan on menniscne lichaman.
 6. <foreign>JU24A/17</foreign> Þy syxtan monðe Johannes fahnode on hys modor
ynnoðe, þa sancta Maria eode in to hys meder Elizabethe.
 8. <foreign>JU24A/20</foreign> Myd þy he getacnode Crist cumenne in þære
clænan fæmnan ynnoð.
 9. <foreign>JU24A/21</foreign> Þæt wæs hræd ærendraca, se tylode to
secganne hys ærndunge ær þon þe he lyfde.
 10. <foreign>JU24A/23</foreign> Ne genyhtsumað ænygum men to asecganne
þæs acennedan engles mægen Johannes.
 13. <foreign>JU24B/1</foreign> On þone ylcan dæg byð <foreign>solstitia</foreign>, þæt
ys on ure geþeode sungihte, forþon ðe seo sunne standeð on mydre lyfte,
swa sanctus Arculfus sagað þæt he gesawe on Hierusalem ane syle on
myddre þære ceastre, seo wæs aseted on þære stowe, þær se
deada man acwycode þa hym man dryhtnes rode ofersette.
 17. <foreign>JU24B/3</foreign> Þonne gelympeð þæt wundorlice on þæs

 18. <foreign>JU24B/7</foreign> Þonne seo sunne byð on þæs heofones mydle,
þonne nafað seo syl nænige sceade.
 20. <foreign>JU24B/10</foreign> Þonne þæs sungihtes beoð þry dagas
forð aurnen, ond se dæg byð hwene scyrtra, þonne hafað seo syl

 21. <foreign>JU24B/13</foreign> Ond swa þa dagas forð onsceortiað, swa byð
þære syle sceade lengra.
 23. <foreign>JU24B/15</foreign> Þeos syl cyþeð þæt Hierusalem seo

þæt ys eorðan nafola, forþam on mydne sumor on mydne dæg scyneð

standeð on mydre eorðan.
 28. <foreign>JU25A/1</foreign> On þone fif ond twentigoðan dæg þæs
monðes byð sancte Lucian tyd.
 29. <foreign>JU25A/2</foreign> Þæt wæs haliges hades fæmne on Rome, ac
heo wæs gehergod fram ælþeodegum cyninge, se wæs on naman Aceia.
 30. <foreign>JU25A/4</foreign> Heo wæs swyðe fæger fæmne.
 31. <foreign>JU25A/5</foreign> Þa wolde se cyning hig gewemman myd hys
fyrenlustum, ond þa cwæð heo to hym, Ic hæbbe mycelne brydguman,
þæt ys Cryst, se gewyrcð raðe mynne teonan on ðe.
 33. <foreign>JU25A/9</foreign> Þa yrsode se cyning wyð hig ærest, ac þa
æt nehstan he ongan hyre arian ond het hyre getymbrian medomlic hus, on
þæt nænig wer næfde ingang, ond he hyre sealde seofon mædeno
þæt hyre þenodon, ond heo þær þeowode gode on fæstenum ond on
gebedum.
 37. <foreign>JU25A/14</foreign> Þonne swa oft swa se cyning wolde feran to
gefeohte wyð hys feondum, þonne ferde he ærest to þysse Crystes
fæmnan ond bæd hig þæt heo for hym gebæde to hyre gode.
 40. <foreign>JU25A/18</foreign> Þonne dyde heo swa.
 40. <foreign>JU25A/18</foreign> Þonne afylde he symle hys fynd ond he com eft ham
symle gesund ond gesygefæsted.
 42. <foreign>JU25A/20</foreign> Þa æfter twentigum gearum þa ætywde
þysse fæmnan heofonlicu gesyhð ond hyre bebead þæt heo ferde eft to
Rome.
 43. <foreign>JU25A/22</foreign> Þa geþrowode heo þær martyrdom for

 44. <foreign>JU25A/23</foreign> Þa eode se cyning to Romeburge gerefan to þam

 46. <foreign>JU25A/25</foreign> Þa frægn se burhgerefa hyne hwæt he
wære.
 47. <foreign>JU25A/26</foreign> Ic eom Aceia, mynre þeode cyning.
 47. <foreign>JU25A/27</foreign> Þa cwæð se gerefa, Hu myht þu for Cryste

 48. <foreign>JU25A/28</foreign> Þa cwæð se cyning, Ic gelyfe þæt mynes

 50. <foreign>JU25A/30</foreign> Ond þa on þære godes andetnysse he geendode

 51. <foreign>JU26A/1</foreign> On þone syx ond twentigoðan dæg þæs

 53. <foreign>JU26A/3</foreign> Hig wæron acennede of Constantines sidan þæs

 55. <foreign>JU26A/6</foreign> Ac Julianus se hæðena casere ongan hig nydan

 56. <foreign>JU26A/8</foreign> Þa hig þæt ne geþafedon, þa sende he hig

bynnan hyra huse, ond he bebead þæt hig man on þam beheafdode, swa
þæt ne wæs nænig tacen hyra cwale ofer eorðan gemeted.
 60. <foreign>JU26A/13</foreign> Þa sona forwearð Julianus se casere.
 60. <foreign>JU26A/14</foreign> Æfter þysum com an stræl of heofonum ond
hyne gewundode on his oðer gewenge, ond he þa swealt sona.
 62. <foreign>JU26A/16</foreign> Ond þæs mannes sunu awedde þe hig ær

 64. <foreign>JU29A/1</foreign> On þone nigon ond twentigoðan dæg þæs

 70. <foreign>JU29A/9</foreign> Þas weras Petrus ond Paulus wæron oft

 73. <foreign>JU29A/13</foreign> Ond on þam cyrcum þe on hyra naman gehalgode

 77. <foreign>JU29B/1</foreign> On þone ylcan dæg byð þæs bisceopes

 78. <foreign>JU29B/2</foreign> He wæs on þære byrig seo wæs haten

 79. <foreign>JU29B/3</foreign> Þæs bysceopes þeaw wæs þæt he sang
æghwylce dæge mæssan gode to lofe myd swyðe mycelre meagolmodnysse
ond myd wependum tearum, ond he wæs swyðe ælmysgeorn.
 81. <foreign>JU29B/6</foreign> Þa ætywde ure dryhten on nyht sumum
mæssepreoste ond hyne het gangan ond secgan þam bysceope þæt he ne
geswyce na þæs þe he to gode dyde, ond he cwæð to hym, Saga hym
þæt he cymð to me æt þæra apostola tyde Petrus ond Paulus, ond
ic hym gylde hys mede.
 85. <foreign>JU29B/12</foreign> Þa ne dorste se mæssepreost þæt þam
bysceope secgan, forþam þe hyt wæs þa þære tyde neah.
 87. <foreign>JU29B/14</foreign> Þa ætywde drihten eft þam mæssepreoste
ond hyne myd wordum þreade ond hyne het secgan þa ylcan word þe he hym
ær bebead.
 89. <foreign>JU29B/16</foreign> Ond þa gyt agælde se mæssepreost hyt ond
hyt hym ne sæde.
 90. <foreign>JU29B/18</foreign> Þa ætywde hym dryhten þryddan syðe ond
hyne þa þreade myd þearlwyslicere swingle for hys ungehyrsumnysse.
 91. <foreign>JU29B/20</foreign> Þa eode se mæssepreost to þam bysceope ond
sæde þæt hym beboden wæs ond onfeold hys hrægl æt hys
sceoldrum ond hym eowde þa læla þære swyngellan þe he from dryhtne
onfeng.
 94. <foreign>JU29B/24</foreign> Þa wæs se bysceop mycle þig reðran on
godum weorcum þe he ymbe þa cuðlican mede gehyrde.
 96. <foreign>JU29B/26</foreign> Þa æfter seofen gearum se bysceop forðferde

 99. <foreign>JU30A/1</foreign> On þone þrytegoðan dæg þæs monðes

 187. <foreign>NO17A/21</foreign> Ond myd swylcere blysse Sancta Hyldan gast wæs

 191. <foreign>NO22A/1</foreign> On þone XXII dæg þæs monðes byð

 193. <foreign>NO22A/4</foreign> Heo wæs gegyred myd hæran æt hyre

 195. <foreign>NO22A/7</foreign> Ond on þære nyhte þa heo wæs in

hyre æfre onhryne myd unclænre lufon.
 198. <foreign>NO22A/11</foreign> Þa gelærde heo þone brydguman þæt he

 200. <foreign>NO22A/13</foreign> Þa he gefullod wæs ond yneode on þone

twegen beagas on hys handa, þa glysnodon hwylum swa rosan blosman, hwylum swa
lilian blostman.
 203. <foreign>NO22A/17</foreign> and þa sealde he oðerne þæra beaga
þære fæmnan and oðerne þam brydguman and cwæð, Healdað ge

godes neorxnawange.
 206. <foreign>NO22A/21</foreign> Þeos fæmne geþrowode martyrdom for Cryste.
 207. <foreign>NO22A/22</foreign> Almatheus hatte Romeburge gerefa.

 208. <foreign>NO22A/24</foreign> Þa heo þæt ne geþafode, þa het he hig

 210. <foreign>NO22A/27</foreign> Þa eode hyre se cwellere to myd sweorde, ond he
hig sloh þrywa myd þam sweorde ond he ne myhte hyre þæt heafod of
aslean.
 212. <foreign>NO22A/29</foreign> Ac heo gebæd hig to þam papan, se wæs
haten Urbanus, ond þa beforan þam papan heo todælde eall þæt hyre
wæs ond hym gesealde ond cwæð to hym, þyssa þreora daga fæc ic
me abæd æt dryhtne þæt ic þe þys sealde, þæt ðu gehalgie
myn hus to cyrcan.
 216. <foreign>NO22A/35</foreign> Ond heo þa onsende hyre gast to gode.
 217. <foreign>NO23A/1</foreign> On þone þreo ond twentigoðan dæg þæs

 218. <foreign>NO23A/2</foreign> Þone Sanctus Petrus sylf gehalgode to papan and

 220. <foreign>NO23A/6</foreign> Þar þes Clementes gedyde þurh hys gebed

 222. <foreign>NO23A/8</foreign> Ond Traianus se casere onsende hys heretogan, se

 224. <foreign>NO23A/11</foreign> Þa ne myhte he hyne oncyrran.
 225. <foreign>NO23A/11</foreign> Þa het he hym gebyndan anne ancran on hys
sweoran ond hyne forsendan on sæ.
 226. <foreign>NO23A/13</foreign> Þa stodon crystene men on þam waroðe ond
weopon, ond þa adruwode seo sæ XXX mila.
 227. <foreign>NO23A/15</foreign> Þa eode þæt crystene folc on þa sæ,
ond hig gemytton þær stænen hus fram dryhtne gegearwod, on þam wæs
geseted Clementes lychama on stænenre earce, ond se ancra þær wæs
big geseted myd þam he wæs ær on þa sæ onsended.
 231. <foreign>NO23A/20</foreign> And æghwylce geare syððan æt hys tyde se
sæ gearwode drigne syðfæt seofen dagas tocumendum mannum to hys
cyrcan.
 233. <foreign>NO23A/22</foreign> Seo cyrce ys on þrym mylum fram þære
eorðan on þære sæ, ond heo ys on easteweardre Ralia mægðe.
 234. <foreign>NO23A/24</foreign> Þær hwylon sum wyf on þære cyrcan
ofergeat hyre cyld slæpende, ond seo sæ fleow ymbe þa cyrcan.
 236. <foreign>NO23A/26</foreign> Þa æfter geares fæce þa þæt folc
eft þyder com to Clementes tyde, þa gemetton hig þæt cyld lyfigende
ond slapende on þære cyrcan, ond hyt ferde myd hys meder.
 239. <foreign>NO23B/1</foreign> On þone ylcan dæg byð þære halgan
wudewan gemynd þære nama ys Felicita.
 240. <foreign>NO23B/2</foreign> Seo þrowode for Cryste myd hyre seofon sunum.
 241. <foreign>NO23B/3</foreign> Heo gelærde þa hyre suna to godes geleafan,
ond heo acende hyg gode myd gaste þa ðe heo myd lychaman on myddangearde
gebær.
 243. <foreign>NO23B/6</foreign> Þeos wyduwe is mare þonne martyre.
 243. <foreign>NO23B/7</foreign> Heo onsende hyre seofen suna to heofena rice, swa
oft heo wæs dead beforan hyre sylfre.
 244. <foreign>NO23B/9</foreign> Heo ondred þæt, gif þa suna ofer hig
lyfedon, ond heo wæs fægnigende þa hig swulton.
 246. <foreign>NO23B/11</foreign> Heo wyscte þæt heo nanne æfter hyre ne
forlete, þe læs, gif hyra hwylc wære hyre oferstealla, þæt se ne
myhte on heofenum beon hyre efngemæcca.
 249. <foreign>NO24A/1</foreign> On þone feower ond twentygoðan dæg þæs
monðes byð sancti Crissogones tyd ond þrowung.
 250. <foreign>NO24A/4</foreign> Se wæs beorht myd eorðlicere æðelnysse
ond wundorlicra on godcundre snytro.
 251. <foreign>NO24A/7</foreign> Þam Crissogone Deoclitianus se casere gehet
ealdordomes medomnysse, gif he wolde forlætan Crystes geleafan.
 253. <foreign>NO24A/9</foreign> Þa cwæð he to þam casere, Ic aworpe þa
myht fram me þe me fram þe gehaten ys swa þæt lam þe ic myd mynum
fotum on trede.
 255. <foreign>NO24A/11</foreign> Ða het se casere hyne beheafdian ond weorpan
þone lychaman ond þæt heafod on sæ.
 256. <foreign>NO24A/14</foreign> Ond þa sum halig mæssepreost feng to þam
lychaman þe þar aworpen wæs to þam waroðe, ond he hyne arweorðlice
bebyrigde, ond eft þurh godes ætywednesse he funde þæt heafod,
þæt hyt seo sæ upwearp, ond he þæt ða bær ond alede hyt to
þam lychaman.
 261. <foreign>NO28A/1</foreign> On þone ehta ond twentygoðan dæg þæs
monðes byð þæs bysceopes þrowung sancti Saturnini.
 262. <foreign>NO28A/3</foreign> Se wæs on þære ceastre þe ys nemned
þolosane, ond þa for þæs bysceopes halignysse geswigdon eall þa
deofolgyld þe hig ær on þære ceastre beeodon.
 264. <foreign>NO28A/6</foreign> and þa syððan forþam yrsodon þa
hæðenan ceastergewaran wyð hyne and gebundon þone halgan bysceop be
þam fotum on sumne fearr ond þone gegremedon þæt he hleop on unsmeðe
eorðan ond þam bysceope þæt heafod tobeot, ond ealle hys lymu wæron
toslytene, ond he þa Criste hys sawle ageaf.
 269. <foreign>NO28A/11</foreign> Ond twa crystene wyf ahyddon þone lychaman under
myclum stangefealle, oð þæt ðæra bysceopa sum þe hys
æfterfyligend wæs getymbrede fægere cyrcan ond on þa þone lychaman
gesette.
 273. <foreign>NO28B/1</foreign> On þone ylcan dæg byð sancti Crisantes tyd
þæs æðelan weres.
 274. <foreign>NO28B/2</foreign> Þone hys yldran befæston on his cnyhthade to
Alexandrea ceastre sumum woruldwysan men þæt he æt þam leornode þa
seofon cræftas on þam beoð gemeted ealle weoruldwysdomas.
 276. <foreign>NO28B/6</foreign> Þæt ys ærest <foreign>arythimetica</foreign>, þæt ys
þonne rymcræft, ond <foreign>astraloia</foreign>, þæt ys þonne tungolcræft, ond
<foreign>astronomia</foreign>, þæt ys tungla gang, ond <foreign>geometrica</foreign>, þæt ys
eorðgemet, ond <foreign>musica</foreign>, þæt ys dreamcræft, ond <foreign>mechanica</foreign>,
þæt ys weoruldweorces cræft, ond <foreign>medicina</foreign>, þæt ys læcedomes
cræft.
 281. <foreign>NO28B/12</foreign> Þa he þas cræftas ealle hæfde
þurhsmeade, þa com he to sumum mæssepreost.
 282. <foreign>NO28B/15</foreign> Þa lærde se hyne godcunde gewrytu.
 283. <foreign>NO28B/17</foreign> Þa forlet he þa woruldgewrytu ond lufode þa
godcundan gewritu ond onfeng fulwyhte ond gode þeowode on clænnysse.
 284. <foreign>NO28B/19</foreign> Þa he þa wæs on þære iugoðe, þa
ongunnon hys yldran hyne laþian to brydþyngum.
 286. <foreign>NO28B/19</foreign> Þa wyðsoc he þam.
 286. <foreign>NO28B/24</foreign> Þa het se fæder gefrætewian sum hus myd
mycelum fægernyssum ond het beran on þæt hus manegra cynna symbel ond
het þone cnyht lædan on þæt hus ond het fif mædenu swyðe
geglengede gangan on þæt hus.
 289. <foreign>NO28B/26</foreign> Þa onhylde se halga cnyht hys ansyne on dune ond
nolde hig na geseon, þe ma ðe V næddran crupon on þæt hus.
 291. <foreign>NO28B/28</foreign> Ond þa sona eode slæp on þa mædenu, ond
hig slepon dæg ond nyht swa lange swa hig on þam huse wæron.
 293. <foreign>NO28B/31</foreign> Þa het se fæder hym gelædan to swyðe
gleawe, seo wæs gefrætwod myd golde ond myd gymmum, þæt seo sceolde
hys geþoht oncyrran, þære nama wæs Darie.
 296. <foreign>NO28B/32</foreign> Þa gelærde he þa to Crystes geleafan, ond
hig lyfedon hym þa samod on clænnysse ond samod hyra lif geendodon on
martyrdome ond samod restað on anre byrgenne, ond þa gastas samod gefeoð
on anum wuldre.
 299. <foreign>NO28B/36</foreign> Ond god dyde þurh hig manege wundru ge þurh
lifigende ge þurh forðfarene.
 301. <foreign>NO30A/1</foreign> On þone þryttygoðan dæg þæs monðes
byð sancte Andreas tyd þæs apostoles.
 302. <foreign>NO30A/2</foreign> He wæs sancte Petres broðer ond he wæs se
æresta dryhtnes þegen ond he ys cweden se wlytega dryhtnes þegen,
forþam ðe he wæs wlitig on lychaman ond he wæs wlitig on mode.
 305. <foreign>NO30A/6</foreign> Ond æfter Cristes upastigennysse he gecyrde twa
mægða to godes geleafan, þa wæron þus genemned, Scyððiam þa
mægðe ond Achaiam þa mægðe.
 307. <foreign>NO30A/9</foreign> Ond on Patria þære ceastre he wæs ahangen
on rode ond myd mycele leohte he onsende hys gast to gode.
 309. <foreign>NO30A/11</foreign> Ond Egeas se ealdorman se þe hyne het ahon þyg
ylcan dæge he wæs fram deofle forbroden ond he sweolt.
 310. <foreign>NO30A/13</foreign> Ond þæs Egeas broðor, se wæs on naman
Stratohles, ond Egeas wyf, þære nama wæs Maximille, hig bebyrigdon
Andreas lichaman myd wyrtgemengnyssum ond myd swetum stencum.
 313. <foreign>NO30A/17</foreign> Ond on Constantines dagum þæs caseres Andreas
lic wæs þanon alæd on þa ceastre þe ys nemned Constantinopolim.
 316. <foreign>NO30A/20</foreign> Þonne se monað byð geendod þe we nemnað
blodmonað, þonne byð seo nyht XVI tida lang, ond se dæg VIII tida.
 318. <foreign>DE00A/1</foreign> On þam twelftan monðe on geare byð an ond XXX
daga.
 318. <foreign>DE00A/2</foreign> Se monað ys nemned on leden Decembris ond on ure
geþeode se ærra geola.
 319. <foreign>DE00A/3</foreign> Forþam þa monðas twegen syndon nemde anum
naman, oðer se ærra geola, oðer se æftera, forþan ðe hyra oðer
gangeð beforan þæra sunnan, ærþon ðe heo cyrre hig to þæs
dæges lenge, oðer æfter.
 323. <foreign>DE10A/1</foreign> On þone teoðan dæg þæs monðes byð
sancta Eulalian þrowung þære fæmnan, seo wæs on þære
mægðe þe ys nemned Hisponia ond on þære ceastre þe ys nemned
Barcilona.
 325. <foreign>DE10A/4</foreign> Seo fæmne wæs XIII geare þa Datianus se
gerefa ferde on þa ceastre crystene men to nydanne fram Crystes geleafan.
 327. <foreign>DE10A/7</foreign> Þa eode þæt mæden hym ongean ond
cwæð, þu godes feond, tohwan gangest þu on þas burh ond tohwan ehtst
þu crystenra manna, ond tohwon tylast þu þæt ðu forleose godes
fæmnan?
 330. <foreign>DE10A/10</foreign> Þa yrsode he ond gebealh hyne ond het hig
aðenian on yren bed ond hig begeotan myd weallende leade, ond hyre þæt
ne geeglode.
 332. <foreign>DE10A/13</foreign> Þa het he hig don on fyrenne ofen, þa ne
gederede hyre þæt.
 333. <foreign>DE10A/15</foreign> Þa het he hys leasere hig behamelian ond hig
þa nacode geunarian.
 334. <foreign>DE10A/17</foreign> Þa cwæð heo, Ic wat for hwæne ic þys
þrowige, efne for Cryst.
 335. <foreign>DE10A/18</foreign> Þa het he hig lædan to beheafdinge.
 336. <foreign>DE10A/19</foreign> Þa cwæð heo to hym, Ic cume eft on
domesdæg ond þe þonne wrege beforan Crystes þrymselte, ond þu
þonne ongitst þu myne ansyne.
 338. <foreign>DE10A/22</foreign> Ond sona swa hig man heafdode, þa com þær
fæger culfre of þam lichaman ond fleah ymbe þone lychaman ond hyne
freode ond þa fleah to heofenum.
 340. <foreign>DE10A/25</foreign> Ond hyre lychama resteð on Barcilonia ceastre.
 342. <foreign>DE13A/1</foreign> On þone XIII dæg þæs monðes byð
sancta Lucian tyd þære æðelan fæmnan.
 343. <foreign>DE13A/2</foreign> Seo wæs on þære mægðe þe ys nemned
Sicilia mægðe ond on þære ceastre þe ys nemned Siracusana.
 344. <foreign>DE13A/4</foreign> Þa þreatode hig þære mægðe ealdorman,
se wæs on naman Fascassius, myd myclum wytum to deofolgyldum ond cwæð
hyre to, Gif þu nelt forlætan þone Crystes geleafan, ic þe hate
lædan to forlegeswifa huse ond þe ðær bysmrian.
 348. <foreign>DE13A/9</foreign> Þa cwæð heo, Nys me þynes weales hæmed
næfre þe leofre þe me nædre toslyte.
 349. <foreign>DE13A/11</foreign> Þa gesealde he þa fæmnan his leaserum ond
cwæð, Bysmriað hig, oð þæt heo dead sig.
 351. <foreign>DE13A/13</foreign> Þa hig þa woldon hig lædan, þa ne myhton
hig nahwyder hig onstyrian.
 352. <foreign>DE13A/14</foreign> Þa eodon heora manege of þæs ealdormannes
þenungwerode.
 353. <foreign>DE13A/15</foreign> Sume sceufon, sume tugon ond swyðe swætton
oð þæt hig geteorode wæron, ond seo godes fæmne hwæðre stod.
 355. <foreign>DE13A/18</foreign> Þa brudon hig rapas on hyre handa ond on hyre
fet ond hig tugon myd þam, ond hig ne myhton hig þa git anne fotlast
furður ateon.
 357. <foreign>DE13A/20</foreign> Þa het se wælgrymma ealdorman hig myd sweorde
wundian on þone ynnoð, ond þa cwæð heo to þam crystenan mannum
þe hyre ymbestodon, þære tyde ys neah þæt godes cyrce hafað sybbe
on eorðan ond crystene men.
 360. <foreign>DE13A/25</foreign> And Dioclitianus, se hæðena casere þe nu
rixað, byð of hys rice aworpen, ond Maximianus his gerefa byð todæge
dead, ond ic beo eower þyngere to gode, gif ge habbað godes geleafan ond
hys wyllan doð.
 363. <foreign>DE13A/29</foreign> Ond se ealdorman þe hig wundian het beforan hyre
eagum wæs gebunden myd ysenum racenteagum ond wæs gelæded to Rome, ond
eall Romana dugoð hyne gedemde to deaðe, and he wæs þær heafde
beheawen, ond hys þæt synnige blod wæs agoten on þa wrace hyre
þæs unsceððian blodes.
 368. <foreign>DE13A/35</foreign> Ond sancta Lucian ær ne gewat, ær hyre com
to godes sacerd ond hyre gesealde husl, ond heo þa hyre to gode gebæd ond
hyre gast ageaf.
 371. <foreign>DE13B/1</foreign> On þone ylcan dæg byð þæs læces tyd
sancti Ursicine, se wæs on Rauenna þære ceastre.
 372. <foreign>DE13B/2</foreign> Þa nydde Paulinus se dema hyne þæt he
sceolde Crystes geleafan forlætan oððe beon beheafdod.
 373. <foreign>DE13B/5</foreign> Þa hyne man lædde to þære beheafdinge,
þa getweode hyne on hys mode ond wolde gecyrran to þam deofolgyldum.
 375. <foreign>DE13B/7</foreign> Þa clypode sum Crystenman ond cwæð,
Ursicine, ær þu hældest oðre men ond nu þu wundast þe sylfne.
 377. <foreign>DE13B/9</foreign> Ond þa gehreow hym þæt hyne æfre swa on
his geþohte getweode, ond he geþrowode martyrdom for Cryste ond gode ageaf
þone deorwyrðan gym þone þe deofol wolde gereafian, þæt ys seo
halige sawl.
 381. <foreign>DE14A/1</foreign> On þone feowerteoðan dæg þæs monðes
byð sancte Hygebaldes gewytennys þæs halgan abbudes, þæs lychama
resteð on Lyndesse mægðe.
 383. <foreign>DE14A/3</foreign> Be þam wrat Beda se leornere on Angelcynnes bocum
þæt he wære haliges lyfes ond swiðe clænes.
 385. <foreign>DE21A/1</foreign> On þone XXI dæg þæs monðes byð sancte
Thomas tyd þæs apostoles, se wæs on Grecisc nemned <foreign>didimus</foreign> ond on
Romanisc <foreign>geminus</foreign>, þæt ys on ure geþeode getwyn.
 387. <foreign>DE21A/4</foreign> Forþam he wæs swa geciged forþam ðe he
wæs urum hælende gelic on menniscre onsyne.
 389. <foreign>DE21A/6</foreign> Ond æfter Crystes upastigennysse he gelærde
monige þeode to Crystes geleafan, Warðwara ond Medware ond Persware ond
Hyrcanas ond Bactrianas ond twa Indea mægðe.
 391. <foreign>DE21A/9</foreign> And he þurhferde hæðenre þeode eorð ond
myddangeardes eastdæl.
 392. <foreign>DE21A/11</foreign> Ond myd Indeum he getymbrede hyra cyninges healle
on heofonum, se wæs on naman Gundaforus, ond þæt geseah þæs
cyninges broðor, þæs sawl wæs on heofenas gelæded myd godes
englum, þæt seo heall wæs getymbred ynnan ond utan myd grenum ond myd
hæwenum ond myd hwytum.
 397. <foreign>DE21A/16</foreign> Ond se wæs eft lyfigende on eorðan se ðe
sæde þæt hyt wære þus getymbred on heofenum.
 398. <foreign>DE21A/18</foreign> Ac on oðre Indea mægðe Mygdæg se cyning
ond hys ealdorman se wæs on naman Caritius, he nydde þysne Thomum þæt
he weorðode sunnan deofolgyld.
 400. <foreign>DE21A/22</foreign> Þær wæs þære sunnan anlycnys geworht
of golde, ond heo wæs on gyldenum scryde, ond æt þam wæron gyldene
hors, ond on þam wæron þa wealdleðer swa upgetiged, swa swa hig urnon
to heofenum up.
 404. <foreign>DE21A/26</foreign> Þa þome þæder ineode, þa eode þær
egeslic deofol ut of þam goldgeweorce ond stod beforan hym, ond þæt
goldgeweorc eall todreas, swa swa weax gemylt æt fyre.
 406. <foreign>DE21A/29</foreign> Þa þæra hæðenra bysceopa sum ofsloh
þone Crystes þegn, ond gewrytu secgað hwylum þæt he wære myd
sweorde þurhstungen, hwylum hig secgað þæt he wære mid sperum
ofsticod.
 409. <foreign>DE21A/33</foreign> He þrowode in Calamina on Indea ceastre, ond hys
lychama wæs alæded of Indeum on þa ceastre þe ys nemned Edyssa.
 411. <foreign>DE21A/36</foreign> Þær he ys geseted on sylfrene cyste, ond seo
hangað on sylfrenum racenteagum.
 412. <foreign>DE21A/37</foreign> Ne mæg þær nænig gedwolman lyfian on
þære ceastre ne nænig þæra þe deofolgyld begangað, ne næfre
syððan ne myhton ælreorde þeode hergian on þa ceastre.

 1. <foreign>MA17A/1</foreign> On ðon seofonteoðan dæg ðæs monðes
martii bið sancte Patrices tyd ðæs halgan bisceopes se gelærde ða
mægðe to geleafan Hiebernia, þæt is scotta mægð.
 4. <foreign>MA17A/5</foreign> His fæder nama wæs Calpurne & his modor
nama wæs conta blata.
 5. <foreign>MA17A/6</foreign> & he sylf wæs on hundteontigum geara & on

 6. <foreign>MA17A/8</foreign> & ær ðam ðe he come on scotta mægðe

Mart 3 (Sweet)
B19.3.
London, British Library, MS. Add. 23211: Sweet 1885, 177-8.



 2. <foreign>AP14A/1</foreign> Mid hiora fiðra flyhte, & se mon ða gelefde
Gode, & he wæs sungen on deað for Criste, & his noma wæs
Maximus.
 4. <foreign>AP18A/1</foreign> On ðone eahtategðan dæg ðæs monðes
bið/ ðæs halgan biscepes tid, sancte Eleutheri, & his modor,
ðære noma wæs sancte Anthiæ.
 5. <foreign>AP18A/3</foreign> He wæs ðære burge biscep ðe is nemned
Mechania, in Apulia ðære mægðe, ah he geðrowade eft in Rome
martyrdom for Criste.
 7. <foreign>AP18A/5</foreign> Adrianus se casere hine ðreatade ðæt he
Criste wiðsoce.
 8. <foreign>AP18A/6</foreign> Ða he ðæt ne walde, ða heht se casere
gesponnan fiower wildo hors to scride, & hine gebundenne in ðæt
scrid/ asetton, ðæt ða wildan hors scealden iornan on hearde wegas in
westenne, & him ða limo all tobrecan.
 11. <foreign>AP18A/9</foreign> Ða cwom Godes engel of hiofonum, & gestillde
ðæm horssum, & hio gelæddon ðæt scrid on hea dune, ðær
him cwom to monigra cynna wildeor, & wunedon mid hine, & ðonne he
hof his hond upp to hiofonum, ðonne hofon ða deor heora fotas upp, &
heredon god mid hine.
 15. <foreign>AP18A/13</foreign> Ða het se casere his huntan hine ðær
gefeccan/ & hine mid sueorde ofslean.
 16. <foreign>AP18A/15</foreign> Ða cwom stefn of hiofonum, & cwæð,
Cym, min ðeow Eleutherius, mine englas ðec lædað in ða hiofonlican
Hierusalem/.
 17. <foreign>AP18A/17</foreign> Ða feoll his modor ufan on his lichoman, &
cwæð, Min sunu, gemyne ðu mec on ðære ecean reste.
 19. <foreign>AP18A/18</foreign> And se casere hio heht gemartyrian.
 20. <foreign>AP21A/1</foreign> ðon ðe he tuelf gear ðær wunode ða eode
he in ðone gefean ðære ecan eadinesse.
 21. <foreign>AP21A/3</foreign> Ðæs æðelwaldes wunder wæs ðæt he
spræc to his liornæra sumum, & ða feringa oðsuigde he, suæ he
hwæshwegu hercnade.
 22. <foreign>AP21A/5</foreign> Ða frægn se his ðegn hine for hwon he suæ
ded, ða cuðæ he, Hu meahte ic bu somod ge in heofon geheran ge her
spræcan.
 25. <foreign>AP23A/1</foreign> On ðone ðrio & tuentegðan dæg ðæs
monðes bið sancte Iorius tid, ðæs æðelan weres, ðone Datianus
se casere seofon gear mid unasæcgendlicum witum hine ðreade ðæt he
Criste/ wiðsoce, & he næfre hine ofersuiðan meahte, & ða
æfter sefan gearum heht he hine beheafdian.
 28. <foreign>AP23A/5</foreign> Ða he ða wæs læded to ðære
beheafdunga, ða cuom fyr of heofonum, & forbernde ðone hæðnan
casere, & alle ða ðe mid hine ær tintergedon ðone halgan wer.
 30. <foreign>AP23A/7</foreign> Ond he sanctus Georgius him to Dryhtne gebæd,
& ðus cuæð, Hælende Crist, onfoh minum gaste & ic ðec
biddo ðæt suæ hwelc mon ðe mine gemynd on eorðan doe, ðonne
afierr ðu from ðæs monnes husum ælce untrymnesse, ne him fiond
sceððe, ne hungor, ne monncwild, & gif monn minne noman nemneð in
ænigre frecennisse, oððe on sæ, oððe on siðfæte, ðonne
gefylge/ se ðinre mildheortnesse.

 2. <foreign>MY02A/1</foreign> On ðone æfterran dæg þæs monðes

 3. <foreign>MY02A/2</foreign> He uuæs biscop in ðære miclan ceastre

 3. <foreign>MY02A/3</foreign> His halignes uuæs foretacnad on his cneahthade.

 13. <foreign>MY03A/4</foreign> Ða Aurelianus se gesið se ðær cualde

 23. <foreign>MY03A/13</foreign> Ðes Sanctus Alexandre uuæs se fifta papa

 24. <foreign>MY03B/1</foreign> On ðone ilcan dæg biþ sio tiid ðæt

 26. <foreign>MY03B/2</foreign> Ðær cuom upp of ðære eorðan wynsumes
stences rec, þær sio rod uuæs gemeted.
 27. <foreign>MY03B/3</foreign> Ðæt treow uuæs aseted ofer deades monnes

uuæs gecyþed þæt ðet uuæs soðlice Cristes rod.
 29. <foreign>MY03B/6</foreign> Ymb þas dagas utan, hwilum ær, hwilum

folc mærsiað letanias, þæt is þonne bene & relicgongas foran

 33. <foreign>MY04A/1</foreign> Gelic agoten fore allum monnum.
 33. <foreign>MY04A/1</foreign> On ðam þrim dagum Cristene menn sceolon
alætan hiera þa woroldlican weorc on ða þriddan tid dæges, þæt

niogoðan tid, þæt is ðonne non.
 36. <foreign>MY04A/6</foreign> Þa dagas siendan ryhtlice to gefæstanne, &
ðara metta to brucanne þe menn brucaþ on ðæt fiowertiges neahta

ætþiowian.
 40. <foreign>MY04A/9</foreign> Ðas þrie dagas siendan monnes saule læcedom

& fulre blisse allra menniscra fionda, forðon þe God us forgifeð his
eorre, gief we ure monnum forgifað.
 45. <foreign>MY05A/1</foreign> On ðone fiftan dæg þæs monðes bið se
dæg þe ure Dryhten on to hiofonum astag.
 46. <foreign>MY05A/2</foreign> Þy dæge hine gesegon nest his þegnas on

 47. <foreign>MY05A/3</foreign> Þy dæge eode sio eorðe in heofon, þæt is

suaþu Dryhnes fotlæsta.
 49. <foreign>MY05A/5</foreign> Ymb þa Dryhtnes fotlæstas timbredon Cristene

 50. <foreign>MY05A/6</foreign> Ond ne meahte sio his suaþu næfre mid

 52. <foreign>MY05A/8</foreign> Gif ðær monn hwæt mennisces on asette,

aswengede on ðære onsion þe ða þer on setton.
 54. <foreign>MY05A/10</foreign> Ðæt dust þæt God þær on træd

 58. <foreign>MY05A/14</foreign> Sancte Arculuos segde þæt ðær ne

Dryhten on stod, he ða to hiofonum astag, ah þæt se weg þær wære
a to hiofonum open.
 61. <foreign>MY05A/17</foreign> Heannes wære oð monnes suioran, &

 64. <foreign>MY05A/20</foreign> Ond Sanctus Arculuos sægde þæt ðær
hongade/ unmæte leohtfæt, & ðæt wære biernende a dæges

 66. <foreign>MY05A/22</foreign> Ond he sægde ðæt æghwelce geare ðy

 73. <foreign>MY05A/28</foreign> Se ondrysnlica wind ðæt deð, þæt se

 74. <foreign>MY05A/30</foreign> Sancte Arculuos sægde þæt he seolf þær

 78. <foreign>MY06A/1</foreign> On ðone sextan dæg þæs monðes bið

 115. <foreign>MY08B/10</foreign> & þa bebead se casere ðæt

 2. <foreign>DE31A/1</foreign> þa he ða ineode on þæt carcern ond hire to
genealæhte, þa com ðider in ursa þæt deor, þæt is on ure
geðeode byren, ond awearp hine to eorðan ond locade to þære godes
fæmnan hwæþer heo sceolde hine cucene þe deadne.
 5. <foreign>DE31A/5</foreign> And þa bebead seo godes fæmne þære byrene
þæt heo læge on þæs carcernes duru, ond heo ongan læran þone
leasere þæt he gelyfde on Crist, ond he þæt geþafade.
 8. <foreign>DE31A/9</foreign> Ond seo byren hine let gangan of þæm carcerne,
ond he þa sona clypode þurh ealle þa ceastre ond cwæð, Se an god is
soð god þone Columbe seo fæmne begangeð, ond nis ænig oþer butan
þam.
 11. <foreign>JA00A/1</foreign> On ðone eahteþan geohheldæg bið þæs
monðes fruma þe mon nemneð Ianuarius, þæt is on ure geðeode se
æftera geola.
 12. <foreign>JA00A/3</foreign> Þæt bið se æresta geares monað mid
Romwarum ond mid us.
 13. <foreign>JA00A/4</foreign> On ðæm monðe bið an ond þritig daga.
 14. <foreign>JA01A/1</foreign> On ðone ærestan dæg þæs monðes bið
Cristes eahteða dæg ond sancta Marian.
 15. <foreign>JA01A/2</foreign> On ðæm dæge Crist onfeng ða ealdan
ymbsnidenysse ond ða ealdan clæsnunge Iudea folces, þæt þonne
wæs þæt hie æghwelcum cnihtcilde ymbsnidon þæt werlice lim on
ðæm eahteþan dæge æfter his acennysse, ond seo clæsnung him
wæs swa halig swa us is fullwiht.
 19. <foreign>JA01A/8</foreign> Ond Crist forðon þa clæsnunge onfeng þæt
he us mid þy getacnode þæt we sceolan aceorfan fram usse heortan
unclæne geðohtas ond from lichoman unalefde dæde, gif we willað
habban lif mid gode.
 22. <foreign>JA01A/12</foreign> Ond on þone eahteþan dæg menn sceopan Criste
naman æfter ealdre wisan.
 24. <foreign>JA01A/14</foreign> Se nama wæs on Iudisc Ihesus ond on grecisc
soter ond on læden saluator ond on ure geðeode hælend.
 25. <foreign>JA01A/16</foreign> Þone naman hæfde se engel sancta Marian
gesæd, ær ðon þe heo geeacnad wære.
 27. <foreign>JA03A/1</foreign> On ðone þriddan dæg ðæs monðes bið
þæs halgan papan tid þe is nemned sancte Antheri.
 28. <foreign>JA03A/2</foreign> He wæs Grecisces cynnes mon, ond he sæt on
sancte Petres setle on Rome þreottyne gear on Maximianus dagum þæs
caseres, ond he geþrowade martyrdom for Criste, ond his lichoma is bebyrged
on ðæm mynstre ðe we nemnað Calistes mynster.
 33. <foreign>JA05A/1</foreign> On ðone fiftan dæg þæs monðes bið
sancte Emelianan tid ðære fæmnan, þæt wæs sancte Gregorius
faðe ðæs þe us fulwiht onsænde.
 35. <foreign>JA05A/3</foreign> Hire ætywde on nihtlicre gesyhðe hire swyster
gast ond cwæþ to hire, Butan þe ic dede þone halgan dæg æt
drihtnes acennisse, ac ic do mid þe ðone halgan dæg æt drihtnes
ætywnesse, þæt is se drihtnes halga twelfta dæg, drihtnes fullwihtes
dæg.
 39. <foreign>JA06A/1</foreign> On ðone sextan dæg þæs monðes bið se
micla ond se mæra dæg þone Grecas nemnað <foreign>Epiphania</foreign>, ond Romware
hine nemnað <foreign>aparitia domini</foreign> þæt is on ure geþeode drihtnes
ætywnesse dæg.
 42. <foreign>JA06A/4</foreign> On ðam dæge he gecyþde mid þæm mæstum
wundrum feowerum þæt he wæs soð god.
 43. <foreign>JA06A/6</foreign> Þæt æreste wundor wæs þæt þreo
tungolcræftegan comon fram eastdæles mægðum to Criste þa þa he
wæs cild, ond him mon brohte gold to gefe.
 45. <foreign>JA06A/10</foreign> On ðæm wæs getacnod þæt he wæs
soð cyning.
 46. <foreign>JA06A/12</foreign> Oðer him brohte recels, on ðæm wæs
getacnod þæt he wæs soð god.
 47. <foreign>JA06A/15</foreign> Se þridda him brohte myrran þa wyrt, on þon
wæs getacnod þæt he wæs deadlic mon, ond þæt he þurh his anes
deað ealle geleaffulle men gefreode fram ecum deaðe.
 50. <foreign>JA06A/17</foreign> Ond on ðone ilcan dæg Crist onfeng fulwihte on
Iordane fram Iohanne þæm fulwere, ond he wæs þa on ðritiges geara
ylde se hælend, þa he þæm fulwihte onfeng.
 52. <foreign>JA06A/19</foreign> Ond on þone dæg æt sumum brydþingum Crist
gecerde sex fatu full wætres to ðæm betestan wine.
 54. <foreign>JA06A/21</foreign> On æghwelc þara fata mihte twegen mittan
oþþe ðreo.
 54. <foreign>JA06A/22</foreign> Ond on ðone ylcan dæg Crist gereorde fif
ðusenda wera of fif hlafum ond of twam fixum, eac wifum ond cildum, þara
wæs ungerim, ond þara hlafgebroca wæs to lafe twelf binna fulle.
 58. <foreign>JA06B/1</foreign> On ðone ylcan dæg bið þæs æþelan
weres þrowung se is nemned sanctus Iulianus, ðæs lichoma resteð in
Antiochia þære ceastre.
 59. <foreign>JA06B/3</foreign> Se sona on his cnihthade ðeowade gode on
clænnesse, ond his yldran hine þa genyddon on his geogoðe þæt he
onfeng æþele bryd, seo wæs on naman Basilissa.
 62. <foreign>JA06B/7</foreign> Ond ða þære forman brydniht, þa hi twa
wæron on ðæm brydbure, þa com þær ærest wundorlic stenc, ond
æfter ðæm stence heofonlic leoht.
 64. <foreign>JA06B/9</foreign> Ond æfter þæm leohte Crist self þær
ætewde mid engla werede.
 65. <foreign>JA06B/11</foreign> Ond ða for þære gesihðe fægernesse ðe
hi gesawon ond ðæm wordum ðe hi gehyrdon hi wunedan a clæne, he mid
werum ond heo mid fæmnum.
 67. <foreign>JA06B/14</foreign> Þes Iulianus awehte hæþenne man of deaðe,
ond se wæs siððan gefullad.
 68. <foreign>JA06B/15</foreign> Se man sæde fram helle siðfæte swylc
sarspell swylce næfre ær on men ne becom ne naht oft siððan.
 71. <foreign>JA06C/1</foreign> On ðone ilcan dæg bið þæs papan tid þe
is nemned ðelesfor, se wæs Grecisces cynnes.
 72. <foreign>JA06C/2</foreign> He sæt on ðæm papsetle ændlefen gear ond
þry monað on þara casere dagum Antonius ond Marcus.
 73. <foreign>JA06C/4</foreign> Ond ðes papa wæs eft Cristes martyr, ond his
lichoma resteð neah sancte Petres lichoman.
 75. <foreign>JA06C/6</foreign> Þes papa gesette ærest manna þæt man
fæste on Rome syfon wucan ær eastran, ond he gesette ærest þæt
man sang gloria in excelsis deo þone lofsang foran to mæssan.
 78. <foreign>JA09A/1</foreign>On ðone nygeðan dæg ðæs monðes bið
sancte Pegean geleornes ðære halgan fæmnan.
 79. <foreign>JA09A/3</foreign> Heo wæs sancte Gutlaces swyster þæs ancran,
ond æfter his geleornisse heo dyde blindum men þæt sealt on eage
þæt he ær gehalgode, ond he mihte sona geseon.
 82. <foreign>JA10A/1</foreign> On ðone teoþan dæg þæs monðes bið
sancte Paules tid.
 82. <foreign>JA10A/2</foreign> Se wæs sextyne geara þa he ærest on þæt
westen gewat, ond he wunade þær oþ þæt he hæfde ðreo ond
hundændleftig wintra.
 84. <foreign>JA10A/4</foreign> Þær he næfre naht oþres ne geseah ne ne
gehyrde butan leona grymetunge ond wulfa gerar, ond æt þæs westenes
æppla ond ðæt wæter dranc of his holre hand.
 87. <foreign>JA10A/8</foreign> Ond ða æt nehstan fedde hine an hræfn sextig

 88. <foreign>JA10A/10</foreign> Ond ða hwæne ær his ende com him to sanctus

 90. <foreign>JA10A/12</foreign> Se Antonius geseah ðæs Paules saule swa hwite
swa snauw stigan to heofonum betweoh engla þreatas ond haligra manna
þreatas.
 92. <foreign>JA10A/15</foreign> Ond twegen leon adulfan his byrgenne on ðæs
westenes sande.
 92. <foreign>JA10A/17</foreign> Þær resteð Paules lichoma mid yfelice duste
bewrigen, ac on Domes dæge he ariseð on wuldor.
 95. <foreign>JA12A/1</foreign> On twelftan dæg þæs monðes bið sancte

 96. <foreign>JA12A/3</foreign> He wæs swiðe æþele for worolde ond micle
æþelra for gode.
 97. <foreign>JA12A/4</foreign> Ond ða he wæs on fif ond twentigum geara, þa

leornade gastlice ðeodscipas.
 100. <foreign>JA12A/7</foreign> Ond he onfeng preosthades scare on ðæs

 101. <foreign>JA12A/9</foreign> Ond he getimbrade on Brytene æþele mynster on

wisdome ge mid woroldlicum frætwum ofersæwiscum ond ða ðæs
æfter sextene gearum þa forlet he þone læmnan ofn ðæs
mænniscan lichoman, ond se gast fleah freo to ðam upplican wuldre.
 108. <foreign>JA13A/1</foreign> On ðone ðreottegan dæg þæs monðes

 109. <foreign>JA13A/3</foreign> Se wæs sancte Martines lareow, ond he awehte

 111. <foreign>JA14A/1</foreign> On ðone feowerteogðan dæg þæs monðes

 112. <foreign>JA14A/3</foreign> Þone rice men hæþne þreadon þæt he
Criste wiðsoce ond hæþengeldum gelyfde.
 114. <foreign>JA14A/5</foreign> A he þæt nolde, he wæs nacod on carcern
onsænded ond þær understregd mid sæscellum ond mid scearpum stanum,
ond þa godes engel on ðære ilcan niht tobrec ðæs carcernes duru ond
hine þonan alædde.
 118. <foreign>JA16A/1</foreign> On ðone sexteoðan dæg ðæs monðes
þonne bið sancte Marcelles tid þæs papan.
 119. <foreign>JA16A/2</foreign> Ðone papan Maxentius, Romeburge ealdormon, nedde
þæt he his fullwihte wiðsoce ond deofolgeldum gelyfde.
 120. <foreign>JA16A/4</foreign> Ða he þæt ne geðafode, þa het he on
ðæs papan ciericean gestællan his blancan ond monig oðer neat, ond he
genydde þone papan þæt he þæm þenade.
 123. <foreign>JA16A/9</foreign> Ond on ðæm ðeowdome he geendade his lif ond
his lichoma resteð arwyrðlice on ðæm mynstre Priscille on ðæm

 126. <foreign>JA16B/1</foreign> On ðone ilcan dæg bið þæs
