 127. <foreign>JA16B/4</foreign> Se wæs acenned in Hibernia mægðe, þæt
is on Scotta lande.
 128. <foreign>JA16B/6</foreign> Þæs gast wæs neahterne of lichoman
alæded, ond he geseah ma ondryrrlices ond eac wuldorlices þonne he mihte
monnum asecgan, ond seo gesihð him wæs on swa micelre gemynde þæt he
on ðæm miclan wintres cele, þonne he ymb þæt þohte oþþe
spræc, ðonne aswætte he eall, ond eft on ðære miclan sumeres
hæte, ðonne he his siðfæt gemunde, þonne ablacode he eall ond
abifode.
 134. <foreign>JA16B/12</foreign> Ond ða ða godes englas eft his gast brohtan to
þæm lichoman, þa locade he on his agenne lichoman swa swa on uncuðne
hræw, ond he nolde næfre eft on ðone lichoman, gif he nyde ne sceolde.
 137. <foreign>JA16B/16</foreign> Þes Fursing gewat eft of Scottum on Brytone, ond
on Eastengla mægðe he getimbrede fæger mynster, þæt is geceged
Cnofesburh.
 139. <foreign>JA16B/18</foreign> Ðæt he dyde on Sigeberhtes dagum þæs
cyninges.
 140. <foreign>JA16B/19</foreign> Ond þanon he gewat ofer sæ in Gallia
mægðe to Clodfeo, Francna cyninge, ond ðær his dagas geendade.
 141. <foreign>JA16B/21</foreign> Ond his lichoma resteð on ðæm tune Ferano,
ond his geearnunga þær wæron oft beorhte gecyþed.
 144. <foreign>JA17A/1</foreign> On ðone seofenteoþan dæg þæs monðes
bið seo geleornes þæs halgan munuces sancte Antonies.
 145. <foreign>JA17A/3</foreign> Se gewat on westen ða he wæs on twentigum
geara, ond on ðæm he wunade, oþ þæt he wæs on fif ond
hundteontigum geara, ond on fruman he þær wunade twentig geara, swa he
nænigne oþerne mon ne geseah.
 148. <foreign>JA17A/7</foreign> Ðær he fæste hwilum twegen dagas, hwilum
þry tosomne, ond ðonne he mete þigde, ðonne wæs þæt hlaf ond
sealt ond lytel wætres drync.
 150. <foreign>JA17A/10</foreign> Ond hine þær deofla costodon mid ofermæte
unclæne luste, efne swa þæt hi eodon on niht to him on geglengedra wifa
hiwe.
 152. <foreign>JA17A/12</foreign> Ðær he geseah eac þone fulan gast þe men
lærð unalyfede lustas.
 153. <foreign>JA17A/14</foreign> Þæt wæs sweart cniht ond lytel ond
egeslic, ond he him sæde sylf þæt his nama wære spiritus
fornicationis, þæt is dernes geligeres gast.
 155. <foreign>JA17A/17</foreign> Hwilum ða deofol hine swungan þæt he ne
mihte hine astyrigean ne noht cweðan.
 157. <foreign>JA17A/19</foreign> Hwilum hi hine bylgedon on swa fearras ond ðuton
eallswa wulfas.
 158. <foreign>JA17A/20</foreign> Hwilum hi him bæron to gold ond seolfer ond him
ætywdon in arwyrðestan hiwe, ond hi him bæran mettas to ond hine
bædon þæt he þa þigde.
 160. <foreign>JA17A/23</foreign> Þonne sænade he hine, þonne glad þæt
deofol ut mid his leasunge swa swa smyc æt his eagdura.
 161. <foreign>JA17A/25</foreign> Antonius wunade on ðæm ytemestan ænde
eorðan ymbhwyrftes on Egypta westenne, ond he wæs hwæþre mære
geond ealne middangeard.
 163. <foreign>JA17A/28</foreign> Ond þa he his dagas geendade, þa ongeatan
þæt his þegnas twegen þæt hine openlice englas læddon to
heofenum, ond his lichoma resteð on ðære miclan ceastre Alexandria.
 167. <foreign>JA17B/1</foreign> On ðone ilcan dæg bið þreora cnihta tid,
þa wæron getwinnas, ond hi wæron nemde sanctus Speosippus ond sanctus
Elasippus ond sanctus Melasippus.
 169. <foreign>JA17B/4</foreign> Þa hæfdon Cristene modar ond hæþenne
fæder, ond þurh heora yldran modor lare hi gelyfdon Gode, ond hwæþre
næron hi na gefulwade, forðon hæðne caseras hæfdon ofslegen ealle
biscopas ond mæssepreostas.
 172. <foreign>JA17B/8</foreign> Þas cnihtas þry fram þrym deman wæron
nedde þæt hi godes geleafan wiðsocan.
 173. <foreign>JA17B/10</foreign> Þa hi þæt ne geþafedon, þa heton þa
deman micel fyr onbærnan ond ða cnihtas ahon on an treow ond byran to
þæm fyre.
 175. <foreign>JA17B/13</foreign> Ða cwædon hi to heora yldran medder, Beo þu
nu ure gemyndig on þinum gebedum.
 177. <foreign>JA17B/15</foreign> Ond þonne þu hlaf brece ond metes onfo,
þonne sæna þu þa cruman for us ðe of þinum beode feallen þæt
we moton bergan of þæs heofonlican cyninges gereordum, þeah ðe we
næron mid fulwihte her on eorðan onðwægen.
 180. <foreign>JA17B/19</foreign> Ða cwæð seo yldre modar, Cnihtas, beoð
orsorge, eower blod eow fulwað, ond eower martyrdom eow gelædeþ to
Cristes gereordum.
 182. <foreign>JA17B/22</foreign> Þa wæron þa cnihtas on ðæt fer
onsænded.
 183. <foreign>JA17B/23</foreign> Ða ne onhran þæt fyr him no, ac hi
onsændon heora gast to gode swa swa þreo lamb.
 184. <foreign>JA17B/25</foreign> Ond seo cierece on þære þe heora lichoma
resteð is neah Lingonabyrig, þa man nemneð æt sanctos geminos, æt
þæm halgum getwinnum.
 187. <foreign>JA18A/1</foreign> On ðone eahtateoþan dæg bið ðære

 190. <foreign>JA18A/5</foreign> On ðy ilcan dæge sancte Peter gehalgode

 192. <foreign>JA19A/1</foreign> On ðone nigonteoþan dæg þæs monðes

 193. <foreign>JA19A/3</foreign> On Dioclitianus dagum þæs hæþenan caseres

 196. <foreign>JA19A/6</foreign> Þa geseah he sittan ðone Halgan Gast on culfran

ond eft fleogan to heofonum.
 198. <foreign>JA19A/10</foreign> Þa gelefde se carcernweard gode.
 199. <foreign>JA19A/10</foreign> Þa het sum hæþen gerefa hi begen belucan on
fyrenum bæþe, ond ymb þreo niht hi eodon gesunde of ðæm.
 201. <foreign>JA19A/13</foreign> Ða gesegon þæt seofon cæmpan, þa
gelyfdon þa for ðæm wundre.
 202. <foreign>JA19A/14</foreign> Þa het se gerefa heora ælcum gebindan leades
bloman on heora swyran ond sændan on wid sæwes grund.
 203. <foreign>JA19A/16</foreign> Þa toburstan þa bendas ond afeoll ðæt

 205. <foreign>JA19A/18</foreign> Ond þa lichoman coman to þam waroðe,
ðær cristene men hi bebyrgdon mid micelre are.
 206. <foreign>JA19A/20</foreign> Ond þær wæron siððan on ðære
stowe monegu wundor.
 207. <foreign>JA19A/21</foreign> Ond se gerefa þe hi cwellan het, se wæs sona
mid swa miclum sare gewitnad, þæt he nolde læng libban, ac he het his
agene men hine sændan on ðone sæ, ond þa sædeor hine sona
forswulgon, þæt his ne com þy furðor an ban to eorðan.
 211. <foreign>JA20A/1</foreign> On ðone twentigþan dæg ðæs monðes
bið sancte Sebastianes tid þæs æþelan martyres, ðone Dioclitianus
se casere, he wæs hæþen, he het hine mid strælum ofscotian, þæt
he wæs ðara swa full swa igl þæt deor bið byrsta, ond mid ðy he
hine ne mihte swa acwellan.
 215. <foreign>JA20A/6</foreign> Ða het he hine mid stengum ðyrcsan oð
þæt he his gast onsende.
 216. <foreign>JA20A/8</foreign> Ond his lichoma wæs gebyrged æt Rome on

 218. <foreign>JA20B/1</foreign> On ðone ilcan dæg bið sancte Fabianes tid

þæt he onfenge Romeburge biscopdome.
 220. <foreign>JA20B/4</foreign> Culfre com fleogan of heofonum ond gesæt ofer
his heafde.
 221. <foreign>JA20B/5</foreign> Ond he hæfde ðære burge biscopdom

 225. <foreign>JA20C/1</foreign> On ðone ilcan dæg bið þara haligra

 227. <foreign>JA20C/4</foreign> Þæs weres nama wæs Marius ond þæs

 230. <foreign>JA21A/1</foreign> On ðone an ond twentigðan dæg bið sancta

 231. <foreign>JA21A/2</foreign> Seo geþrowade martyrdom for Criste þa heo

 232. <foreign>JA21A/4</foreign> Þa fæmnan Simfronius, Romeburge gerefa, ongan

 233. <foreign>JA21A/5</foreign> Þa heo þæt nolde, þa het he hi nacode
lædan to sumum scandhuse, þær hire brohte godes engel swylcne gerelan,
swylcne næfre nænig fulwa, þæt is nænig webwyrhta, þæt mihte
don on eorðan.
 236. <foreign>JA21A/9</foreign> Ðæs burhgerefan sunu wolde ræsan on hi on
ðæm scandhuse ond hi bysmrian, ac fram deoflum forbroden he aslat.
 238. <foreign>JA21A/12</foreign> Þa cwædon Romware þæt heo wære
dryegge ond scinlæce, ond hire man bestang sweord on ða hracan, ond ðus
heo onsende hire gast to Gode.
 240. <foreign>JA21A/15</foreign> Ond hire lichoma resteð neah Romebyrig on
ðæm wege þe hi nemnað Numentana.
 242. <foreign>JA21A/16</foreign> Ond naht lange æfter hire þrowunge heo
ætywde hire yldrum on midde niht þær hi wacedon æt hire byrgenne,
ond heo cwæþ to him, Ne wepað git me na swa ic dead sy, ac beoð me
efenbliðe, forðon þe ic eom to Criste on heofonum geþeoded ðone ic
ær on eorðan lufade.
 247. <foreign>JA22A/1</foreign> On ðone twa ond twentigðan dæg þæs
monðes bið sancte Vincentes ðrowung þæs diacones, se þrowade in
Hispania ðære mægðe on ðære ceastre Falentia.
 249. <foreign>JA22A/4</foreign> Þær Datianus se casere nydde Valerium þone
biscop ond ðone ylcan diacon Vincentium to hæþenscipe.
 251. <foreign>JA22A/6</foreign> Þa swygode se biscop.
 251. <foreign>JA22A/6</foreign> Ða cwæþ se diacon to þam biscope, Clypa
ongen þissum deofles hunde þe þe on beorceð.
 252. <foreign>JA22A/8</foreign> Þa het se casere forlætan ðone biscop ond
ðone diacon miclum witum underþeodan, ac ne mihte he mid nænge þara
hine acwellan ne hine genydan þæt he Criste wiðsoce, ac he mid micelre
blisse ðone sigefæstan gast to gode onsænde.
 256. <foreign>JA22A/13</foreign> Ond se casere þa bebead þæt hine man
forlete unbyrgedne, þæt hine fuglas ond wilde deor forswulgon.
 258. <foreign>JA22A/16</foreign> Ða com þærto blæc fugel, hæfde micele
feðra, ond swift, se adraf ealle þa oþre fuglas ond þa wildan deor fram
þæm lichoman.
 259. <foreign>JA22A/18</foreign> Ða het se casere hine wurpan on wid sæ.
 260. <foreign>JA22A/19</foreign> Ða ferede hine godes hand þider þær hine
cristne men siððan a wulderlice aredon.
 262. <foreign>JA22B/1</foreign> On ðone ilcan dæg bið þæs halgan weres

 264. <foreign>JA22B/3</foreign> Ond Cossra, Persida cining, hine het ahon be

 265. <foreign>JA22B/6</foreign> Þa he þæt ne geðafade, þa het se cining
hine beheafdian.
 266. <foreign>JA22B/7</foreign> Þa Heraclius se casere genam his lichoman mid

 269. <foreign>JA22B/11</foreign> Ond þær mon byrð his heafod on ðas dagas

 271. <foreign>JA23A/1</foreign> On ðone ðreo ond twentigðan dæg bið

 275. <foreign>JA23A/6</foreign> Ond þa sona com þunerrad ond legetsleht ond

 276. <foreign>JA23A/8</foreign> Ond hire lichoma resteþ on ðære ylcan

 279. <foreign>JA24A/1</foreign> On ðone feower ond twentigðan dæg þæs

 280. <foreign>JA24A/3</foreign> Se biscop mid cristene folce forstod cirican duru a

 282. <foreign>JA24A/5</foreign> He cwæþ to him, Ne gang þu na on godes hus,
ðu hafast besmitene handa ond þu eart deofles wulf.
 283. <foreign>JA24A/7</foreign> Ond þa het se kasere hine beheafdian ond his

 285. <foreign>JA24A/10</foreign> Ond ðara cnihta naman wæron Urbanus,

 288. <foreign>JA25A/1</foreign> On ðone fif ond twentigðan dæg þæs

 496. <foreign>MA23A/1</foreign> On ðone ðreo ond twentegðan dæg ðæs

 499. <foreign>MA23A/4</foreign>    Hi wæron swa gescæpene ðæt hi ne

 500. <foreign>MA23A/6</foreign> Ne hi ne mihtan næfre forealdian ne deade beon,

 503. <foreign>MA23A/10</foreign> Adam lifde her on wræcsiðe nigan hund geara

 508. <foreign>MA23B/1</foreign> On ðone ylcan dæg bið þæs halgan

 509. <foreign>MA23B/2</foreign> Se þrowade monigfealdne martyrdom for Criste on

 737. <foreign>AP27A/4</foreign> Ac heo gelyfde gode þurh sancte Georgius lare
ðæs martyres.
 738. <foreign>AP27A/5</foreign> Ða se casere ðæt ongeat þæt heo Criste
gelyfde, þa cwæð he, Wa me, Alexandree, þu eart beswicen mid Georgius
scinlacum.
 740. <foreign>AP27A/8</foreign> Forhwon toweorpest þu min rice oþþe tohwon
forlætest þu me?
 741. <foreign>AP27A/9</foreign> Þa he þa ne mihte hi mid his wordum oncerran,
þa het he hi ahon be hire loccum ond hi þreagean mid missenlicum witum.
 743. <foreign>AP27A/12</foreign> Ða he þa ne mihte mid þæm hi
oferswiðan, þa het he hi lædan to beheafdianne.
 745. <foreign>AP27A/14</foreign> Ða bed heo þa cwelleras ðæt hi hire
geanbidedan medmicle hwile.
 746. <foreign>AP27A/15</foreign> Þa eode heo on hire palatium þæt is on hire
healle, ond anhof hire eagan upp to heofonum ond cwæð, Geseoh, drihten,
þæt ic forlæte nu mine healle opene mid eallum minum goldhordum for
þinum ðæm halgum naman.
 749. <foreign>AP27A/20</foreign> Ac ðu, min hælend, ontyn me nu þin
neorxnawong.
 750. <foreign>AP27A/21</foreign> Ond ða gefylde heo hire martyrdom mid Cristes
geleafan.
 752. <foreign>AP28A/1</foreign> On ðone eahta ond twentegðan dæg ðæs
monðes bið sancte Vitales tid þæs martyres, se resteþ on Vicolonge,
þæt is, on ðæm langan tune.
 754. <foreign>AP28A/3</foreign> Se wæs ærest caseres cæmpa under Paulino
ðæm deman on Rauenna ðære ceastre, ac he þa gelyfde on Crist ond
oðre men lærde to Cristes geleafan.
 756. <foreign>AP28A/6</foreign> Þa yrsode se dema forþon ond hine þa nydde to
deofolgylde begonge.
 757. <foreign>AP28A/8</foreign> Þa he þæt ne geþafode, þa het se dema
adelfan deopne seað ond hine cwicne on ðone ansændan ond hine fyllan
ufon mid eorðan ond mid stanum, oþ þæt he his gast onsænde.
 760. <foreign>AP28A/11</foreign> On ðære stowe wæron oft siððan
heofonlico wundro.
 762. <foreign>AP28B/1</foreign> On ðone ylcan dæg bið sancte Cristofores
ðrowung þæs miclan martyres.
 763. <foreign>AP28B/2</foreign> Se com on Decies dagum þæs caseres on ða
ceastre þe Samo is nemned of þære þeode þær men habbað hunda
heafod ond of þære eorðan on ðære æton men hi selfe.
 765. <foreign>AP28B/6</foreign> He hæfde hundes heafod, ond his loccas wæron
ofer gemet side, ond his eagan scinon swa leohte swa morgensteorra, ond his
teþ wæron swa scearpe swa eofores tuxas.
 768. <foreign>AP28B/9</foreign> He wæs gode geleaffull on his heortan, ac he ne
mihte sprecan swa mon.
 769. <foreign>AP28B/11</foreign> Ða bæd he god ðæt he him sealde monnes
gesprec.
 770. <foreign>AP28B/12</foreign> Ða stod him æt sum wer on hwitum gegirelan
ond eðode him on ðone muð.
 771. <foreign>AP28B/13</foreign> Ða mihte he siððan sprecan swa mon.
 771. <foreign>AP28B/14</foreign> Ða sænde se casere twa hund cæmpena
þæt þa hine gelæddan to him.
 772. <foreign>AP28B/16</foreign> Gif he þonne nolde to him cuman, þæt hi
hine ofslogon ond him brohtan þæt heafod to þæt he gesege hu lic
þæt wære.
 774. <foreign>AP28B/18</foreign> Ða ða cempan him to coman, ða ne dorstan hi
no him genealæcean, ond þa hwæþre ferde he mid hin.
 776. <foreign>AP28B/20</foreign> Þa he þa com to þæm casere ond he geseah
his onsyne, þa wundrade he swa ðæt he feoll of his ðrymsetle.
 777. <foreign>AP28B/22</foreign> Ða bead se casere him gold ond seolfor ðæt
hine oncerde fram Cristes geleafan.
 779. <foreign>AP28B/24</foreign> Þa he þæt ne geþafade, þa het he hine
tintergian mid missenlicum witum.
 780. <foreign>AP28B/26</foreign> Ða he þa ne mihte mid þæm hine
oferswiðan, ða bebead he þæt hine mon lædde to beheafdunga.
 782. <foreign>AP28B/28</foreign> Ða gebæd Cristoforus him to drihtne ond
bæd god ðæt æghwelc ðara manna þe his reliquia aht hæfde,
þæt he næfre hi fordemde on heora synnum, ne þæt godes yrre ofer
hi come, ne him wære hwæs gneaðes ne oþerra worldwisena.
 785. <foreign>AP28B/33</foreign> Þa com stefn of heofonum, ond seo cwæð, Swa
hit bið swa swa þu bidest.
 786. <foreign>AP28B/34</foreign> Ond ic þe soðlice secge.
 787. <foreign>AP28B/35</foreign> Gif hwilc man on micelre neadþearfnesse bið
þin gemyndig, ond he geceð him to geþingum ðinne ðone medoman naman,
ic þonne gefremme þæs mannes nedðearfnesse.
 789. <foreign>AP28B/38</foreign> Ða geendode Cristoforus his martyrdom.
 790. <foreign>AP28B/39</foreign> Ða gebohte an biscop his lichoman mid feo, se
wæs on naman Petrus, ond hine gelædde on his ceastre ond hine gesette
æt sumum mere, of þæm fleow ær flod ond gehwerfde ða ceastre.
 793. <foreign>AP28B/43</foreign> Ond siððan wæs seo ceaster wið þæm
flode gehealden on godes wuldor.
 795. <foreign>AP28B/46</foreign> Þonne se monað bið geendad ðe we nemnað
eastormonað, þonne bið seo niht tyn tida lang ond se dæg XIIII tida.
 797. <foreign>MY00A/1</foreign> On þone fiftan monað on geare bið an ond
þritig daga.
 797. <foreign>MY00A/2</foreign> Se monað is nemned on læden Maias ond on ure

on Germania lande, of ðæm Ongla ðeod com on þas Breotone, þæt hi
on þæm monðe þriwa on dæge mylcedon heora neat.
 802. <foreign>MY01A/1</foreign> On ðone ærestan dæg þæs monðes bið

 803. <foreign>MY01A/3</foreign> His nama is gereht on læden os lampadis,
þæt is on ure geþeode leohtfætes muþ.
 804. <foreign>MY01A/5</foreign> He getacnað ða gastlican lareowas godes

 805. <foreign>MY01A/6</foreign> Ure hælend geceas ðysne Philippum him to
þegne on Galilea mægðe fram Bethsaida ðære ceastre.
 807. <foreign>MY01A/8</foreign> Bethsaida is gereht domus venatorum, ðæt
þonne is huntena hus.
 808. <foreign>MY01A/9</foreign> Ðes Philippus æfter þæs hælendes

 809. <foreign>MY01A/11</foreign> Ðær he awehte ðry men of deaðe, ond his

 813. <foreign>MY02A/1</foreign> On ðone æfteran dæg þæs monðes bið

 816. <foreign>MY02A/5</foreign> Ðære burge biscop ær him wæs nemned

 816. <foreign>MY02A/6</foreign> Se sæt sume symbeldæge on ðære cierecan,

 819. <foreign>MY02A/9</foreign> Ða ongan he fullwian ða oðre cnihtas on

 820. <foreign>MY02A/11</foreign> Ond þa sona het se biscop ðone cniht him to

snyttro gefylled.
 823. <foreign>MY03A/1</foreign> On ðone ðriddan dæg þæs monðes bið

 826. <foreign>MY03A/4</foreign> Þa Aurelianus se gesið, se þær cwealde

 827. <foreign>MY03A/6</foreign> Ða hi þæt ne geðafodon, þa het he sendan

 828. <foreign>MY03A/8</foreign> Ða nolde hi þæt fyr bærnan.
 829. <foreign>MY03A/9</foreign> Þa het he þa mæssepreostas beheafdian ond
ðone papan ofstician.
 830. <foreign>MY03A/10</foreign> Ða sona com stefn of heofonum, ond seo
cwæþ, Aurelianus, ðysum monnum þe þu her bismrodest, him is godes

 832. <foreign>MY03A/14</foreign> Ða swealt he sona þære ilcan niht mid
egeslice deaðe, ond his wif, seo wæs on naman Seueriane, heo bebyrgde
ðæs papan lichoman ond þara mæssepreosta arweorðlice on þære
seofoðan mile fram Romebyrg on ðæm wege Numentana.
 836. <foreign>MY03A/19</foreign> Ðes sanctus Alexander wæs se fifta papa
æfter sancte Petre.
 838. <foreign>MY03B/1</foreign> On ðone ilcan dæg bið seo tid þæt
Cristes rod wæs gemeted ærest, swa us þa halgan gewritu secgað, on
ðone dæg þe we nemnað quinta nonas Maius.
 840. <foreign>MY03B/4</foreign> Ðær com upp of ðære eorðan wynsumes
stences rec ðær seo rod wæs gemeted.
 841. <foreign>MY03B/6</foreign> Ond ðy ilcan dæge þe seo rod wæs gemeted
þæt treow wæs geseted ofer deades mannes lichoman, ond se sona aras,
ond þurh ðæt wundor wæs gecyþed þæt þæt wæs soðlice
Cristes rod.
 845. <foreign>MY04A/1</foreign> Ymb þas dagas utan, hwilum ær, hwilum
æfter, beoð þa þry dagas on ðæm godes ciricum, ond Cristes folc
mærsiað letanias, þæt is þonne bene ond relicgongas, foran to
Cristes uppastignesse.
 848. <foreign>MY04A/5</foreign> On ðæm ðrym dagum sceolon cuman to godes
cirican ge weras ge wif, ge ealde men ge geonge, ge þeowas ge ðeowenne to
ðingianne to gode, forðon ðe Cristes blod wæs gelice agoten for eallum
monnum.
 851. <foreign>MY04A/9</foreign> On ðæm þrym dagum cristne men sceolon
alætan heora ða woroldlican weorc on ða þriddan tid dæges, ðæt
is on undern, ond forð gongen mid þara haligra reliquium oð ða
nigeðan tid, þæt is þonne non.
 854. <foreign>MY04A/14</foreign> Ða dagas syndon rihtlice to fæstenne, ond
þara metta to brucenne ðe menn brucað on ðæt feowertiges nihta
fæsten ær eastran.
 856. <foreign>MY04A/16</foreign> Ne bið alefed on ðyssum dagum ðæt mon
blod læte oððe a clæsnungdrenceas drince oððe aht feorr gewite
for woroldlicre bysgunge fram ðære stowe ðe he sceal gode
ætþeowian.
 858. <foreign>MY04A/20</foreign> Ðas ðry dagas syndon mannes sawle læcedom
ond gastlic wyrtdrenc.
 860. <foreign>MY04A/22</foreign> Forðon hi sendon to healdanne mid heortan
onbryrdnesse, þæt is mid wependum gebedum ond mid rumedlicum ælmessum
ond fulre blisse ealra mænniscra feonda, forþon ðe god us forgyfeð his
erre, gif we ure monnum forgeofað.
 864. <foreign>MY05A/1</foreign> On ðone fiftan dæg þæs monðes bið se
dæg þe ure dryhten to heofonum astag.
 865. <foreign>MY05A/2</foreign> Ðy dæge hine gesegon nyhst his þegnas on
Oliuetes done.
 866. <foreign>MY05A/3</foreign> Ðær he bletsade hi, ond ða gewat mid þy
lichoman on heofonum.
 867. <foreign>MY05A/5</foreign> Ðy dæge eode seo eorðe on heofon, ðæt
is se mon ofer engla ðrym, ond on Oliuetes dune syndon nu gyt ða swæþe
dryhtnes fotlasta.
 869. <foreign>MY05A/8</foreign> Ymb þa drihtnes fotlastas timbredon cristne men
seonewealte cirican wunderlice.
 870. <foreign>MY05A/9</foreign> Ne mihte seo his swaðu næfre mid nænigre
oðre wisan beon þæm oðrum florum geonlicod ond gelice gehiwad.
 872. <foreign>MY05A/12</foreign> Gif þær mon hwæt mænnisces on asette,
ðonne seo eorðe him onufan scealde ðeah hit wære marmarstanas, ða
wæron aswengde on ðara onsyn þe þær on sæton ðæt dust
ðæt god ðær on træd ond þa his swaða ðe þær onþricced
sendon, ða syndon monnum to ecre lare, ond dæghwamlice geleaffulle men
nimað ðæt sand, ond þær hwæðre ne bið nænig wonung on
þæm sande ðære drihtnes fotswaða.
 878. <foreign>MY05A/20</foreign> Sanctus Arculfus sæde þæt þær ne
mihte nænig hrof on beon on ðære cirican on ðære stowe ðe ure
drihten onstod þa he to heofonum astag, ac þæt se weg ðær wære a
to heofonum open þara monna eagum þe him þær gebædan on ðære
ylcan stowe.
 882. <foreign>MY05A/26</foreign> Ond he sæde þæt þa drihtnes fotlastas
wæron beworht mid ærne hweole, ond þæs heanes wære oð monnes
swyran, ond þæt þær wære ðyrel on middum þæm hweole, ðurh
þæt mihton men ufan beorhtlice sceawian drihtnes fota swaðe, ond
þæt hi mihton mid heora handum ræcean ond niman þæs halgan dustes
dæl.
 887. <foreign>MY05A/33</foreign> Ond sanctus Arculfus sæde þæt þær
hangade uþmæte leohtfæt, ond ðæt wære a byrnende dæges ond
nihtes ofer þara drihtnes fota swaða.
 889. <foreign>MY05A/36</foreign> Ond he sæde þæt æghwelce geare ðy
dæge æt Cristes uppastignesse on middes dæges tide, æfter þon
þe mæssesangas wæron geendode on þære ylcan cirican, þæt
þær to come þæs strongestan windes yste, ond þæt se swa
stronglice hrure on þa circan, þæt þær ne mihte nænig mon
ænge gemete on ðære circean oððe on hire neahstowe gestandan
oþþe gesittan, ac þæt ealle þa men ðe þær þonne wæron
lagon aþænede on þære eorðan mid ofdune healdum ondwleotan, oþ
þæt seo ondrynslyce yst forð geleoreð.
 897. <foreign>MY05A/47</foreign> Se ondrysnlica wind þæt deð þæt se
dæl ðære ciricean ne mæg habban ðone hrof ðær þæs
hælendes fotlastas syndon under.
 899. <foreign>MY05A/50</foreign> Sanctus Arculfus sæde þæt he self ðær
wære ondweard æt þære ylcan cyricean ðy dæge æt Cristes
uppastignesse, ða se stranga ond se forhtlica wind þær onræsde.
 902. <foreign>MY06A/1</foreign> On ðone sextan dæg þæs monðes bið

 904. <foreign>MY06A/5</foreign> Þæm Eadberhte wæs gewunelic þæt he

þæt is ær geolum, þæt he wunode on dygolre stowe on his gebedum

 908. <foreign>MY06A/10</foreign> Ond seo stow wæs ymburnen mid sæs streamum.

 912. <foreign>MY06A/15</foreign> Ða bæron hi þæs lichrægles dæl to

 919. <foreign>MY06A/25</foreign> He cwæð, Ic wat cuðlice þæt seo stow

 922. <foreign>MY06A/30</foreign> Ða noht longe æfter þissum ða geuntrumade

 932. <foreign>MY08A/1</foreign> On ðone eahteþan dæg þæs monðes bið

 944. <foreign>MY08B/13</foreign> Ða cwæþ he to þæm þe hine læddon,

 946. <foreign>MY08B/17</foreign> Þa bebead se casere þæt nænig mon þone

 948. <foreign>MY08B/21</foreign> Ða coman þyder tu wilddeor ond heoldon ðone

 952. <foreign>MY09A/1</foreign> On ðone nygeþan dæg ðæs monðes bið

 955. <foreign>MY10A/1</foreign> On ðone teogþan dæg ðæs monðes bið

 1318. <foreign>JY07B/28</foreign> Ond gif hwilc mon sie on ondyrstlecum wisum, ond

 1390. <foreign>JY15A/25</foreign> Drihten, gif hwilc mon hæbbe micle scylde, ond

 1393. <foreign>JY15A/28</foreign> Ond gif hwilc mon wille feran ofer sæs yþe,

 1395. <foreign>JY15A/31</foreign> Ond gif hwilc mon sy from deofle geswenced, ond
he cyme to cyrican ond him þær gebidde on minum noman, sele þu, dryhten,

 1842. <foreign>AU29A/2</foreign> Ðone het Herodes beheafdian, forðon þe he

 1846. <foreign>AU29A/8</foreign> Forhwon wolde se ælmihtiga god þæt sanctus

ænig mon ne mæg monum areccan?
 1854. <foreign>AU29A/18</foreign> Forþon Herodes het beran þæt heafod on

 1948. <foreign>SE08B/1</foreign> On ðone ylcan dæg byþ þæs bisceopes

 1979. <foreign>SE14B/1</foreign> On ðone ylcan dæg biþ sancte Ciprianes tid

 1981. <foreign>SE14B/4</foreign> Galerius se aldorman, beforan him he het arædan

 2021. <foreign>SE15B/29</foreign> Ða gefullde he ðæt cild ond þa demde

 2025. <foreign>SE16A/1</foreign> On ðone XVIan dæg þæs monþes bið

se ðeow wære se ðe fenge on kyninges quene to unryhtum hæmde.
 2066. <foreign>SE21A/21</foreign> Ond ða sona æfter Matheus þrowunge þa

ond he asette his sweord upweard ond ða hyne sylfne ofstang.

 2266. <foreign>OC18C/25</foreign> Ða on mergen com se biscop þæder ond þa

to cirican ond hit ðær asetton.
 2269. <foreign>OC18C/28</foreign> Ond ðær georn XVI wintre mæden to
ðære bære, seo wæs blind acenned, ond heo meahte sona geseon.
 2271. <foreign>OC19A/1</foreign> On ðone XVIIII dæg þæs monðes bið
sancta Pilagian geleornes þære godes þeowenne.
 2272. <foreign>OC19A/2</foreign> Seo wæs æryst mima in Antiochia þære
ceastre, þæt is scericge on urum geðeode.
 2273. <foreign>OC19A/4</foreign> Seo glengde hi swa þætte noht næs on hyre
gesewen buton gold ond gimmas, ond eall hyre gyrela stanc swa ælces cynnes
ricels.
 2275. <foreign>OC19A/7</foreign> Þa gecyrde heo æne into cirican þær
Nonnus se biscop sægde godspel be ðam toweardan godes lombe.
 2277. <foreign>OC19A/9</foreign> Ða weop heo sona swa ðæt hyre fleowon þa
tearas of ðam eagum swa swa flod, ond ða ðy ilcan dæge gesohte heo
þone biscop ond cwæð to him, Ic eom deofles ðinen.
 2280. <foreign>OC19A/12</foreign> Ic yðgode mid synnum swa sæ mid yðum.
 2280. <foreign>OC19A/13</foreign> Ic wæs synna georn, ond in deaðlicum
listum.
 2281. <foreign>OC19A/14</foreign> Ic wæs beswicen ond ic beswac monige þurh
me.
 2282. <foreign>OC19A/15</foreign> Ac gefulla me þæt mine synna syn adilgode.
 2283. <foreign>OC19A/16</foreign> Þa gefullode se biscop hy ond hyre gesealde
husl, ond æt ðam fulwihte hyre onfeng sum godes þeow þære noma
wæs Romana.
 2285. <foreign>OC19A/19</foreign> Þæs ða ymb twegen dagas, þær heo slep
æt ðære godmodor huse, þa com hyre deofol to ond hy awehte ond
cwæð to hyre, Min hlæfdige, gif ðe wæs gold to lytel oððe
seolfor oððe deorwyrðra gimma oððe ænigra woruldwelena, ic
ðæt sona gebete, ac ne forlæt me.
 2289. <foreign>OC19A/24</foreign> Ða cwæð heo, Ic ðe wiðsace, forðon
ic eom nu in Cristes bure.
 2290. <foreign>OC19A/26</foreign> Þa on ðære eahtoðan nihte hyre fulwihtes
þa gegyrede heo hy mid hærenre tunecan ond mid byrnan þæt is mid
lytelre hacelan, ond heo næs na leng ðær gesewen, ac heo gewat on
Oliuetes dune ond hyre timbrede lytle cytan in ðære stowe þe Crist him
gebæd þa he wæs mon on eorðan.
 2294. <foreign>OC19A/31</foreign> Þær hio wunode þreo gear, þæt
nænig mon wiste hwæðer hio wæs wer ðe wif, ærðon ðe heo
forðfered wæs.
 2296. <foreign>OC19A/33</foreign> Ða onfand se biscop on Hierusalem þær he
hyre lichoman gyrede þæt heo wæs wif.
 2297. <foreign>OC19A/34</foreign> Ða cwæð he, God, þe sy wuldor.
 2298. <foreign>OC19A/36</foreign> Ðu hafast monigne haligne ofer eorðan
ahyded.
 2300. <foreign>OC21A/1</foreign> On ðon XXI dæg þæs monðes bið
þæs halgan fæder geleornes sancti Hilariones.
 2301. <foreign>OC21A/2</foreign> Se wæs upcymen in Palistina mægðe in ðam
tune ðe is nemned Ðabata, ond he wæs sona on his cnihthade on gewritum
gelæred.
 2303. <foreign>OC21A/5</foreign> Ond he gewat in westen þa he wæs XVI
wintræ, ond þær hyne dioflu costodon in mislicum hywum.
 2305. <foreign>OC21A/7</foreign> Hwilum hy him raredon on swa hryðro, hwilum hy
him lægon big swilce nacode wifmen, hwilum hy æteowdon him swa swa
þeotende wulf, hwilum swa beorcende fox, ond he ðæt eall oferswiðde
þurh Cristes miht ond dyde unrim heofonlicra wundra.
 2309. <foreign>OC21A/12</foreign> Ðara wæs sum þæt sum geong mon bæd
sume gode fæmnan unrihthæmedes.
 2310. <foreign>OC21A/14</foreign> Þa heo þæt ne geþafode, ða agrof se
mon on ærenum brede drycræftæs word ond bedealf under þone
þerscwold þæs huses þær seo fæmne ineode. ond þa sona swa heo
ineode, þa wæs heo of hyre ryhtgewitte.
 2313. <foreign>OC21A/18</foreign> Ac heo cleopode to ðam geongan be his naman.
 2314. <foreign>OC21A/19</foreign> Þa gelæddon yldran hy to sancti Hilarione.
 2314. <foreign>OC21A/20</foreign> Þa hrymde ðæt deoful in ðære
fæmnan ond cwæð to him, þu me nedest to utgonge, ond ic ne mæg,
buton me se geonga læte se me under ðam þerscwolde geband.
 2317. <foreign>OC21A/23</foreign> Þa cwæð se godes wer to ðam deofle,
Tohwon eodest ðu in ðis godes mægden?
 2318. <foreign>OC21A/25</foreign> Forhwon noldest ðu gongan in ðone mon þe
ðe in hy sende?
 2319. <foreign>OC21A/26</foreign> Þa cwæð ðæt deofu, he hæfde minne
geferan in him, ðæt deofol ðe hyne lærde ða unclænan lufan.
 2321. <foreign>OC21A/28</foreign> Ða geclænsode se Godes wer ða fæmnan
for ðon scindlacum.
 2322. <foreign>OC21A/29</foreign> Ða sanctus Hilarion wæs on <foreign>LXXXm</foreign> wintrum,
þa he forðferde.
 2323. <foreign>OC21A/31</foreign> Ond þy dæge þe he geleorde, he cwæð
to him sylfum, Gong ut, sawl, hwæt drædest ðu ðe?
 2325. <foreign>OC21A/32</foreign> Gong ut, hwæt tweost ðu ðe nu?
 2325. <foreign>OC21A/33</foreign> Hundseofontig geara þu þeowodest gode, ond nu
gyt þone deað þe ondrædest?
 2326. <foreign>OC21A/35</foreign> Ond æt ðissum worde he onsende his gast, ond
his lichoma is in Palestina mægðe in ðære stowe þa hatte Maiuma.
 2329. <foreign>OC24A/1</foreign> On ðone XXIIII dæg þæs monðes bið
ðæs martyres tid þrowung sancti Genesi, ðone mon acwealde, forðon
ðe he nolde deofulgild weorðian.
 2331. <foreign>OC24A/3</foreign> Þæs gemynd is mycel on twam burgum on twa
healfa þæs flodes ðe hatte Rodanum, þæt is on ure geðeode Rodena
mere.
 2333. <foreign>OC24A/6</foreign> In oðre birg is seo stow þe he mid his blode
gehalgode þa hyne mon martyrode, in ðære birg is his lichoma geseted.
 2335. <foreign>OC24B/1</foreign> On ðone ilcan dæg bið XVI cempena tid, ða
het Claudius se casere heafde beceorfan in ðære ceastre Figligna,

 2337. <foreign>OC24B/4</foreign> Ond hie wæron bliðran to ðam deaðe
þonne hy her on hæðengilde lifden.
 2338. <foreign>OC24B/5</foreign> Þara cempena <foreign>IIII</foreign> wæron nemned þiosius

 2340. <foreign>OC26A/1</foreign> On ðone XXVI dæg þæs monðes bið

 2341. <foreign>OC26A/2</foreign> He wæs Ceaddan broðor, ond sum halig mon

 2343. <foreign>OC26A/5</foreign> Ceadde wæs biscop in Eastseaxum, ond

 2346. <foreign>OC28A/1</foreign> On ðone XXVIII dæg þæs monðes þara

 2347. <foreign>OC28A/2</foreign> Simonis wæs sancta Marian swystorsunu, Cristes

 2349. <foreign>OC28A/5</foreign> Þonne wæs Thaddeos oðer noma Iudas.
 2349. <foreign>OC28A/6</foreign> Ðas apostolas æfter Cristes upastigenesse

 2352. <foreign>OC28A/9</foreign> Þær hy gedydon ðæt cild sprecende
þæt ne wæs anre nihte eald.
 2353. <foreign>OC28A/11</foreign> Simones lichoma resteð on ðam lande Bosfore,

 2356. <foreign>OC28B/1</foreign> On ðone ilcan dæg bið sancta Cyrillan

 2357. <foreign>OC28B/2</foreign> Seo wæs Decies dohtor þæs caseres, ac
Claudius se casere hy nydde þæt heo deofolgild herede.
 2358. <foreign>OC28B/4</foreign> Þa heo ðon wiðsoc, ða het he hy mid
sweorde ofstingan ond hyre lichoman weorpan hundum.
 2359. <foreign>OC28B/6</foreign> Ða Iustinus se mæssepreost genom þone
lichoman on niht ond bebyrigde mid oðrum halgum monnum.
 2362. <foreign>OC31A/1</foreign> On ðone XXXIan dæg þæs monðes bið
sancti Guintines ðrowung þæs martyres.
 2363. <foreign>OC31A/2</foreign> Se com of Rome in Galwalas in ða ceastre
Ambeanis, ðær Riciouarus se gerefa mid miclum witum hyne nydde to

 2365. <foreign>OC31A/5</foreign> Ða he ðæt ne geðafode, ða het he hyne

 2366. <foreign>OC31A/6</foreign> Fleah on ðam lichoman culfre swa hwit swa snaw,
ond seo fleah to heofenum.
 2367. <foreign>OC31A/8</foreign> Ða het se gerefa weorpan his lichoman in ða ea
ðe Sumena is nemned, ond þæt heafod þærto.
 2369. <foreign>OC31A/10</foreign> Ond æfter <foreign>LV</foreign> geara godes engel getæhte

 2371. <foreign>OC31A/13</foreign> Ond ða gebead heo hyre on ðam ofre.
 2371. <foreign>OC31A/13</foreign> Ða ahleop se lichoma sona up of ðam

 2373. <foreign>OC31A/15</foreign> Ond se lichoma stanc ond þæt heafod swa

 2374. <foreign>OC31A/17</foreign> Ond þæt wif heo ða arwyrðlice bebyrgde,
ond ealle ða untruman men þa ðe þyder comon to hy wæron sona hale.
 2376. <foreign>OC31A/20</foreign> Þonne se mona bið geendod ðe we nemnað
winterfylleð, þonne bið seo niht XIIII tida long, ond se dæg tyna.
 2378. <foreign>NO00A/1</foreign> On ðam endlyftan monðe on geare bið XXX
daga.
 2378. <foreign>NO00A/2</foreign> Se monoð is nemned on læden Novembres ond on
ure geðeode blodmonað, forðon ure yldran, ða hy hæðenne wæron
on ðam monðe hy bleoton a, þæt is þæt hy betæhton ond
benæmdon hyra deofolgyldum ða neat þa ðe hy woldon syllan.
 2382. <foreign>NO01A/1</foreign> On ðone ærystan dæg þæs monðes
bið ealra haligra tid.
 2382. <foreign>NO01A/2</foreign> Þa tid æryst gesette Bonefacius se papa on
Rome, mydþy þe he on ðone dæg gehalgode to cirican sancta Marian ond

Pantheon.
 2385. <foreign>NO01A/6</foreign> In ðam Romane guldon ða hy hæðene
wæron eallum heora deofolgyldum, ond siððan hy cristene wæron, hy
ðær weorðedon eallra haligra gemynd.
 2388. <foreign>NO01A/9</foreign> Ond se papa ða bebead þæt æghwylce geare
se dæg in godes ciricum in cristenum folcum wære on swylcre arwyrðnesse
swylce se ærysta dæg in natale domini, þæt is ærysta
geohheldæg.
 2391. <foreign>NO01B/1</foreign> On ðon ilcan dæg bið þæs diacones tid
sancti Cesari, se ðrowode martyrdom on Aurelianus dagum þæs caseres.
 2393. <foreign>NO01B/3</foreign> Ðone Leontinus se ealdormon het adrencan in
strongum streame for Cristes geleafan.
 2394. <foreign>NO01B/5</foreign> Ond þæt wæs gewrecen on ðone ilcan
dæg.
 2395. <foreign>NO01B/6</foreign> Se ealdormon rad þurh sumne wudu.
 2395. <foreign>NO01B/6</foreign> Þa ræsde an næddre of holum treowe æt
ðam healsetan him on ðone bosm ond hyne toslat þæt he wæs sona
dead.
 2398. <foreign>NO01C/1</foreign> On ðone ilcan dæg bið þæs
mæssepreostes ðrowung sancti Benigni.
 2399. <foreign>NO01C/2</foreign> Se com from eastdæle on Galwala mægðe ond
eardode in ðam tune þe hatte Spaniaca.
 2400. <foreign>NO01C/4</foreign> Ða het Aurelianus se casere hyne mid witum
þreatian from Cristes geleafan.
 2401. <foreign>NO01C/5</foreign> Ða he þæt ne geþafode, þa het he hyne
belucan in carcerne VI dagas ond VI niht ond XII gehyngrede hundas mid him
þæt he wære from ðam tobroden.
 2404. <foreign>NO01C/9</foreign> Ða wæron him ða hundas milde for godes
egesan ond his na ne onhrinon.
 2405. <foreign>NO01C/10</foreign> Ða ðy VIan dæge het se casere him forslean
þone sweoran.
 2406. <foreign>NO01C/12</foreign> Ða sona com fleogan of ðam carcerne snawhwit
culfre, ond seo fleah to heofenum.
 2407. <foreign>NO01C/13</foreign> Ond ðær com to ðam lichoman swyðe wynsum
stenc ond eac fyrhto mid.
 2408. <foreign>NO01C/15</foreign> Ond sum Cristen wif on niht genam ðone lichoman
ond hyne arwyðlice bebyrgde, ond æt ðam wæron siððan oft
heofonlico mægen.
 2411. <foreign>NO06A/1</foreign> On ðone VI dæg þæs monðes bið
þæs abbodes geleornes sancti Wunnoci.
 2412. <foreign>NO06A/2</foreign> He wæs ðæs mynstres hlaford ðe be suðe
sæ is nemned Wurmhol, ond he wæs hwæðere swa eaðmod þæt he
wolde wyrcan æghwylc ðara weorca þe ðam oðrum broðrum wæs heard
ond hefig.
 2415. <foreign>NO06A/6</foreign> Ond æt nehstan þa he ealdode ond he ne myhte
ute wyrcan, þa wolde he grindan mid his halgum hondum þam broðrum to mete
Cristes þam þearfendum.
 2417. <foreign>NO06A/9</foreign> Ða sona þa he þære cweorna nealæhte
ond þæt corn þær onlægde þa orn seo cweorn ðurh godcunde miht,
ond se abbod beleac ða duru ond stod be ðære cweorna ond song his
gebedu.
 2420. <foreign>NO06A/13</foreign> Ða æt nehstan wæs ðær swylc
genihtsumnes meluwes ðæt hy ðæt ealle wundredon hwonon þæt
come.
 2422. <foreign>NO06A/15</foreign> Ða sume dæge an ðara broðra locode in
ðæt hus þurh an lytel ðyrel.
 2423. <foreign>NO06A/16</foreign> Þa gestod seo cweorn sona, ond se mon
ablindode.
 2424. <foreign>NO06A/18</foreign> Ond hyne ða oðre swiðe afyrhte þanon
læddon, ond he sægde þam broðrum þæs mynstres ðæt wundor
þæt he ðær geseah.
 2426. <foreign>NO06A/20</foreign> Ond ða oðre dæge onleat he wepende to
ðæs abbodes fotum ond him bæd forgifnesse, ond ða gebletsode se abbod
his eagan on dryhtnes naman, ond he myhte sona geseon.
 2429. <foreign>NO07A/1</foreign> On VII dæg þæs monðes bið wintres
fruma/.
 2429. <foreign>NO07A/2</foreign> Se winter hafað tu ond hundnigontig daga, ond
ðonne gongað þa VII steorran up on æfen ond on dægered on setl.
 2432. <foreign>NO08A/1</foreign> On ðone eahtoðan dæg þæs monðes
bið ðara martyra þrowung þe we nemnað on gewritum quattuor
coronatorum, þæt is þara gesigefæstan weras feower, þara naman
wæron Claudius, Castorius, Simfonianus, Nicostratus.
 2435. <foreign>NO08A/5</foreign> Ðæt wæron <foreign>IIII</foreign> stancræftigan in
Rome.
 2436. <foreign>NO08A/6</foreign> Þær wæs samod VI hund cræftigena ond
XXII ond næron nane oðre him gelice.
 2437. <foreign>NO08A/8</foreign> Hy gesenedon ælce morgen heora iserngeloman,
ond ðonne næron hy na tobrocene, ac hy grofen æghwylcne stan swa se
casere geðohte.
 2439. <foreign>NO08A/11</foreign> Ða wæs ðara cræftigena on naman an
Simplicus.
 2440. <foreign>NO08A/12</foreign> Ða lyfde se goda ond fulwihte onfeng, ond ða
siððan dyde he eall ðæt ða oðre dydon.
 2441. <foreign>NO08A/13</foreign> Þa sealde god þissum V cræftegum maran
gyfa þonne ðam oðrum.
 2442. <foreign>NO08A/15</foreign> Ða wregdon ða oðre cræftigan hy to ðam
casere ond sægdon him þæt hy wæron Cristene, ond þæt hy þurh
drycræft dydon ða cræftlican weorc, for ðe hy þa weorc senodon mid
Cristes rode tacne.
 2445. <foreign>NO08A/19</foreign> Þa yrsode se casere ond het hy cwice belucan in
leadenum cistum ond ða weorpan in flod.
 2447. <foreign>NO08A/21</foreign> Ond ða æfter XLIIm daga sum cristen mon
ateah ða cista up mid þam lichoman ond asette in his hus, ond siððan
wæron monegu wundru ðurh ðas halgan weras geworden.

Mart 6 (Henel)
B19.6.
London, British Library, MS. Harley 3271: Henel 1934-5, 347.



 2. <foreign>MY09A/1</foreign> Sumor hafað hundnigantig daga, þonne gangað
þa seofan steorran on uhtan upp and on æfen on setl.
 4. <foreign>NO07A/1</foreign> Winter hafað twa and hundnigantig daga, þonne
gangað þa seofon steorran upp on æfen and on dægred on setl.
